Typhoon Lands in Western Fujian: Positive and Negative Centers Merge, Wind Intensifies; Coastal Areas Along the River Will Experience Strong Winds and Rain 23

(Nanjing) Central Meteorological Information: After the typhoon landed in Xiamen for the second time on the 6th, it reached northern Guangdong on the morning of the 7th, changed direction to the northeast, and moved to the western part of Fujian Province in the afternoon, between 116 degrees east longitude and 25 degrees north latitude. Due to the occurrence of a negative center in its south on the 6th, and the subsequent merger of the positive and negative centers, the wind intensified on the 7th. It is currently moving northeast at a speed of 20 kilometers per hour, and will accelerate further. It is expected to reach the lower reaches of the Yangtze River within the day. Strong winds and rain will occur in the coastal area of the East China Sea and the lower reaches of the Yangtze River. (7th Central Telegram)

(Xiamen) The hurricane subsided on the morning of the 7th, but there was still wind, followed by heavy rain, intermittent. The night was still filled with dense clouds. Ships in the inner harbor resumed navigation on the morning of the 7th. Transportation between Quanzhou, Xiamen, Zhangzhou, and Xiamen resumed. There was heavy rain in Zhangzhou and Quanzhou on the 6th and 7th. If it does not clear up, there is a high risk of a third disaster. Furthermore, in this Anxi flood, over two thousand houses collapsed throughout the county, and over a hundred people died. The area of Dabu in Yongchun County was also affected, with over a hundred houses collapsing, but not as severely as in An'nan and Jinjiang. (7th Special Telegram)

Shaoxing: In opposition to the foil monopoly, a large number of foil workers destroyed the residence of Director Qi of the Foil Tax Bureau and the foil shops of the monopolized company on the 7th. In the afternoon, the province ordered the suspension of registration, and the county government announced temporary martial law. (7th Special Telegram)

Wu Wentian Arrives in Nanjing to Report on Attending the International Labor Conference 25

(Nanjing) Wu Wentian, advisor to the International Labor Conference, arrived in Nanjing on the morning of the 7th to report to Chen Gongbo on his attendance. Representative Wang Jinxia is expected to arrive on the morning of the 8th. (7th Central News Agency Telegram)

Judicial Yuan Clarifies Doubts Regarding Punishment of Banditry Cases 26

(Nanjing) The Judicial Yuan recently decided that in cases involving bandits, if the provincial government's approval for execution was granted before the abolition of the Regulations for the Punishment of Banditry, the original judgment should be executed unless there are grounds for extraordinary appeal or retrial. If the approval was granted after the abolition of the regulations, the approval is immediately invalid and should be handled according to the usual procedures of criminal procedure. (7th Central News Agency Telegram)

Secretary of the Economic Commission Water Conservancy Association, Liu Zongwu, Discusses the Recent Situation of the Yellow River in Shandong 28

(Nanjing) Liu Zongwu, Secretary of the Economic Commission Water Conservancy Association, returned to Nanjing on the evening of the 6th after inspecting the dike construction in Shandong. On the 7th, he told reporters that there had been frequent heavy rains in Shandong recently, and the Yellow River water had become increasingly turbid and violent. Five or six breaches had gradually merged into one, and most of the water was overflowing from there. Recently, it has gradually encroached on various railway lines, and there is a risk of traffic arteries being cut off. Dike closure work is currently underway, but the lack of materials has slowed down the project. The disaster situation in Shandong is severe this time, and it will be difficult to recover within ten years. (7th Central News Agency Telegram)

Ministry of Finance Improves Nitre and Sulfur 29

(Nanjing) Since the Ministry of Finance took over the nitre and sulfur affairs, it has been working hard to rectify them. The nitre part includes the Bianlian Nitre Factory, which purchases raw nitre for refining. The sulfur part has been improving the quality and reducing the cost in the three provinces of Hunan, Hubei, and Henan, which have the highest production. It has also established an improved sulfur refining experimental field in Xin'an, Henan, using the latest scientific methods to improve manufacturing. Furthermore, since there are currently no factories in China manufacturing potassium chlorate, the Ministry has established a research committee to be responsible for research and development. Currently, the Ministry considers sulfuric acid, a type of nitrate mineral, to be in great demand domestically. The Shanghai Kaicheng Acid Manufacturing Company and the Tianjin Lizhong Acid Factory have abundant production capacity, and the Ministry has ordered the Nitre and Sulfur Bureaus of various provinces and relevant agencies to promote its purchase and use. The reduction amount for third-class will then be used to reduce the first and second class fares accordingly. Currently, the PingSui Railway and other lines have drafted plans and submitted them to the Ministry. After all the railways have submitted their plans, they will be reviewed and approved, and then implemented on a specific date. As for whether to adopt the freight rate system of "decreasing with distance" for passenger transport in the future, the Ministry of Railways is currently studying it. This principle of "decreasing with distance" can be adopted for passenger transport, but it should be implemented after collecting opinions from various railways. (7th Special Telegram)

Italian Troops Steadily Heading to Africa; Using Air Force to Win; Intensifying Training of New Aircraft; Using Poison Gas Bombs When Necessary; National Armed Forces Number 900,000 56

(Rome) Although Italy has deployed a large number of land forces, its government still hopes to win in the war against Abyssinia by using the air force. Special new high-speed aircraft are currently being trained in Sicily. These new aircraft can carry 500 two-pound bombs filled with tear gas, lethal gas, or special fragmentation bombs. It is reported that at the start of the war, the Italian army plans to use 400 aircraft carrying tear gas bombs to launch a fierce aerial assault to subdue the Abyssinian army. If this fails, it plans to use poison gas bombs. However, in consideration of global public opinion and humanitarianism, it does not want to use this lightly if it can be avoided. Besides this, Italy is unwilling to antagonize the Abyssinian people by other means, as it wants to establish a colony in the future and live in harmony with the Abyssinian people. The Italian army is now equipped with specially made lightweight gas masks. The Fiat factory has now started producing 50 high-speed aircraft for practice and will produce another 200. All of them are equipped with two engines, and the speed can reach 300 miles per hour. According to Italian newspapers, although Italy is sending a large number of troops to serve in the colonies, it has also compiled new divisions to serve in the country in place of the troops that have been sent out. The recent mobilization order has sent two divisions of regular troops and one division of Blackshirts, totaling 70,000 people, to Africa. As of now, the total number of armed forces in Italy is approximately 900,000. Italy is still able to form new divisions without having to call up more levels of reservists. Therefore, the remaining reservists of the 1912 class are planned to be called up in the future and are not intended to be called up at present. There are currently seven divisions of regular troops, totaling 100,000 people, who have been sent to serve in Africa. Most of them have already set out. Six divisions of Blackshirts, totaling approximately 80,000 people, have also been ordered to go to Africa. In addition, there are two divisions of Eritrean soldiers, totaling 30,000 people, and 10,000 regular troops originally stationed in the colony. Therefore, the number of Italian troops prepared for combat currently reaches 220,000, and there are at least 15,000 specialists, etc., who are traveling with the army, but not as many as with the air force, because Mussolini aims to first attack Abyssinia with aircraft and achieve a quick victory. The Italian authorities have received the London Gazette, stating that the Italian female ambassador to England has met with many retired British officers, soldiers, engineers, doctors, and nurses, all of whom are willing to serve Italy in wartime. The Italian ambassador expressed gratitude to them and sought instructions from the government. (6th Reuters Telegram)

(Rome) News here today: Italy currently has a large army of 225,000 people, some of whom have already left for East Africa, and some of whom are also preparing to leave. Currently, Italy has armed 925,000 people, 700,000 of whom will be stationed domestically. In addition, there are 340,000 Fascist troops, and 200,000 conscripts from the 1912 class who can be mobilized at any time. (6th National Telegram)

Italian Eritrea: Rushing to Build Military Roads; Soldiers on Expedition Die One After Another Due to Unacclimatization 58

(Paris) Abyssinian King A sat at his desk in the lower level of a special new palace, filled with documents and telegrams, and met with a special Reuters reporter. Except for the reporter, no one else was present. King A, dressed in a gorgeous black shirt, apologized to the reporter for receiving guests in this attire, saying that the situation was serious and he had no time to think about clothing. The reporter continued to ask whether the King would accept any form of economic control of Abyssinia by the League of Nations. Therefore, I should not refuse this kind of assistance. Those who are familiar with the situation in our country know that if war breaks out, Abyssinia is not in danger. The Abyssinian government is now considering implementing special plans to protect the lives and property of foreigners in the event of war or troop movements. The reporter asked if the King would be willing to meet with Italian Prime Minister Mussolini in Italy or Abyssinia. The King replied that no one has proposed this suggestion yet. If there is one, I will certainly consider it. The King also told the reporter that although he is determined to do everything in his power to maintain peace, if Italian troops invade Abyssinian territory, he intends to lead the people to fight bravely. The King now works 18 hours a day and is very well-informed about current events. Leaders of tribes from all over the country now come to the palace to see him every day, all stating that they are willing to be loyal to the King and serve him, and asking for supplies of arms and ammunition. The King is now doing his best to supply them, but it is no secret that Abyssinia currently lacks various weapons. Italian Crown Prince to be Promoted to General 63

Inspection of Flood Conditions on Rivers, Special Correspondent of this Newspaper, Geng Ya: One Night in Huangjia Bridge 64

Zhongxiang County, upstream of Shayang, with the breaching of the Three Gorges Lion's Mouth, has already caused disaster to Tianmen, Hanchuan, and other counties, turning them entirely into a watery expanse. However, the flow is merciless, rushing in all directions, causing considerable damage to Zhongxiang itself. According to investigations, the major disaster in the county occurred on the night of July 6th (the further upstream, the earlier the flood season, and the disaster telegrams received by the provincial government also follow the water source order, upstream first and then downstream). Gale-force winds and torrential rain continued all night. The next day, the dikes and embankments below Jiangjia Temple successively collapsed, with floodwaters pouring into the city, instantly reaching depths of several feet. The county government building was flooded up to the eaves, and all land tax documents were lost. Residents fled without escape, with countless deaths. The collapse of houses was even more countless. Further up the river, places like Yicheng, Xiangyang, Gucheng, Guanghua, Jun County, Yun County, and Yunxi, all counties within the Xiang River basin, were all disaster areas of the Xiang River floods. Only the severity of the disaster varied slightly. The reporter originally planned to travel along the river to Xiangfan, then take the Xiang (Yang) Hua (Yuan) Road to the Pinghan Railway north, but above Shayang, boats cannot sail. The inland waterway navigation operated by the Hubei Provincial Construction Department only sails to Shayang. If switching to smaller boats, it would not only take more time, but the security of the waterways above Zhongxiang is also quite questionable. In the end, I changed my route from Shayang to Yuekou, disembarked, and detoured to Tianmen for inspection, then returned to Hankou and went directly north on the Pinghan Railway.

When the boat sailed from Shayang to Yuekou, it went downstream very quickly. It was noon, and I often saw groups of three or five people on the street looking up at the sky, mumbling and sighing in fear. The reporter also looked up with the crowd and suddenly saw a star in the middle of the sky, which, even under the daylight, still shone brilliantly in all directions. After the heavy rain, the weather was clear, or it might have been that the star's orbit was in a certain position. Therefore, it could suddenly be seen in broad daylight. The people on the street did not understand and made wild guesses about disasters. The thought was probably stimulated too deeply by the floods, which led to a case of being scared by shadows.

Yuekou is forty li from Tianmen. Originally, it was a land route, but after the major disaster, it required both land and water travel. I first hired a rickshaw to travel along the winding paths. The vegetable gardens and soybean fields passed had once been flooded in low-lying areas. Because it was a flood, it had neither the benefit of rain nor the harm of silty wasteland. There had been no rain for the past two weeks, and the blazing sun was raging, causing the ground to crack and the crops to wither. Farmers were working hard to draw water, some by hand and some by foot. The sounds of the water wheels arose everywhere in the fields, no different from a tragic cry of drought coming after the flood. Others weeding were in teams of more than ten, wearing straw hats and holding long hoes, sitting or standing, hoeing and retreating. The operation was very laborious, but the pace was quite relaxed. From time to time, I heard high-pitched farming songs, saying, "...Farmers don't see money from farming, while wealthy city dwellers can't finish eating. Alas, the dragon turns over, the sky connects to the water, the water connects to the sky, and ninety thousand out of one hundred thousand farming households are running out of food. Let's go, let's go, alas, don't let go of the hoe, alas, eat Hankou first, alas, then go down to Yangzhou, alas..." The singing method was one person singing alone in front, with everyone singing in chorus behind, the melody tragic and the lyrics clear and audible.

That day was extremely hot and windless. The temperature must have been above 100 degrees Fahrenheit. The ridges of the fields and the dikes were rugged and uneven. I got out of the car to walk. When encountering slopes, the car could not climb, so I had to carry it with the rickshaw puller. Because I had luggage, I could not send the car away to go alone, resulting in being drenched in sweat. Farmers and passersby mostly took shelter in the shade of trees. Nearby, villagers provided hot tea for people to drink freely. After passing by and resting briefly, I heard them chatting, saying that Yuekou was the only place in Tianmen County spared from the disaster, thanks to the heroic efforts of the stationed troops in rushing to rescue the situation. There were two parts of the stationed troops, one belonging to the 105th Division, which did not boast of its merits or brag about its abilities, and the people greatly respected and appreciated them. The other belonged to the ×× Division, which had taken the opportunity to extort money from the people. Although they have now worked hard to rescue the situation and achieved results, in the hearts of the people, the shortcomings still outweigh the merits. Furthermore, Commissioner and Tianmen County Magistrate Shi Yuling, some people had seen him with muddy feet supervising the work of rushing to rescue the situation, and they praised him unanimously as a good official. As the ancients said, what the people hear is what Heaven hears.

Fifteen li to Jie River, with a population of about five or six hundred families, living on a high and long embankment, supposedly a regular market. However, the goods sold did not include cloth or grain, mostly small stalls with snacks, such as fried dough sticks and cooked tofu. Those selling pigs all pierced their left ears with thick ropes, which was quite different from the methods of bundling the four hooves in North China and caging the entire body in Guangdong and Guangxi. But the ultimate goal was the same: to drive these dull creatures, raised fat and lazy, to the slaughterhouse. Walking through the embankment street, I stopped to look into the distance. The vast expanse of water in front was unknown for hundreds of miles. Villages where the sounds of chickens and dogs could be heard in the past were now scattered and floating like sandy islands. Fertile fields that were once connected by paths are now turned into ponds and ditches where fish and shrimp chase each other. At that time, Wu, the chief of the second district of Tianmen, was directing boatmen to rush to transport sacks to the city. According to him, "The disaster situation in that district, such as Songjia River Ridge, Li Jiawan, Yanglin Jiawan, Luotai Jiawan, Xin Jiawan, and Zhong Jiawan, all experienced a two-zhang rise in water overnight. The disaster situation is extremely tragic. According to investigations, more than 360 houses have been completely washed away, 140 men and women have died, and 420,000 mu of fields have been flooded. In Songjia River Ridge village, with a population of more than 100 families, only three houses remained after the flooding, blocked by willows. Most of the villagers who were saved were also washed and hung on high branches."

Buying a boat to go to the city, no one responded to Wu's offer to hire a small boat at a high price. It was still a returning boat carrying bamboo and wood. It was not until we were paddling in the water (actually paddling over the fields) that I learned that a few days ago, two men and a woman hired a small boat and, in the middle of the journey, suddenly drew their knives and killed the boatman, seizing the boat and fleeing. The boatman was a father and son. The son died, and the old man was pushed into the water. They then hit the old man with an oar, but the oar broke without hitting him. The old man pretended to be dead to escape. In the dark night, he called for help and returned to chase. The stolen boat was difficult to maneuver with only one oar. Seeing the chasing boat approaching, they fled into the reeds and were eventually captured. They were then shot in the county. The woman was a kidnapped disaster victim from Mianyang and is currently imprisoned. Since this incident, everyone has been warned not to hire laborers or boats for longer distances. To think that someone would have murderous intent for a small boat worth a dozen yuan, killing and being killed, a total of three lives lost, is also regrettable. However, due to the impact of the flood, unexpected tragedies may not be limited to this. As the ancients said, after a major disaster, war is likely to break out. Prevention is key, and all places should have taken note of this.

When the boat first set off, the trees seen had large branches and trunks, hanging with furniture and old clothes washed away by the water, swaying and scattered, much like the colorful masts erected in a theatrical stage. Those with lush branches and leaves and short trunks were all lying prostrate in the flood, drifting like algae. After passing five or six villages, the remaining empty houses and rafters were inhabited by waterbirds. When the boat arrived, they flew away in a disorderly manner. The ground was covered with rubble and the smell of rotting grass. The odor was like garbage but not garbage, like a fish market but not a fish market, making people nauseous and unbearable for a moment. The graves around the village were numerous, gradually appearing above the water, but many coffins had been exposed, making the scene even more desolate. The setting sun sank into the water, and the sky turned dark. I vaguely saw someone waving a fan in a village house. The boatman said that it was still three or four li from the city, and it was not convenient to proceed in the dark on a non-official waterway. He invited me to spend the night at his house, the place where I vaguely saw someone waving a fan. The village was called Huangjia Bridge, and landing on shore made the darkness even more intense due to the loss of reflection from the water surface. Huangjia Bridge was a fishing village by the river, with eight or nine households. Only three families who had fled the disaster had returned. None of them lit lamps. The boatman's wife had already prepared dinner in the open air. I was invited to eat with them. There were several earthenware bowls. The boatman pointed to them with his chopsticks one by one and said, "There are only four things: chili peppers, mashed broad beans, purslane, and thin millet porridge. There is no oil or salt, and it is tasteless. I am afraid it will make you suffer." After dinner, neighbors came to talk, eagerly asking whether Hankou had escaped danger and when the breached dikes would be repaired. Later, the boatman asked his wife to sleep on the boat while he accompanied the reporter to sleep in the room. The four walls had been washed down by the water. Only the rear part had a bamboo bed, tied to the beams and pillars of the house with ropes to a large stone mortar (a heavy tool for pressing grain). Therefore, it was not washed away. The weather was extremely hot and humid. The boatman advised, "There is no one else in the house. You may as well take off your clothes and sleep. If you have valuables, you can put them under your pillow." Although this came from good intentions, the special environment increased the reporter's fear, so I dared not close my eyes all night. There was no wind or waves in the night, and all was silent, except for the chirping of autumn insects, like playing mourning music for the disaster victims. The bedroom was empty, and when I faintly saw the east turn white, I immediately ordered him to get up and row the boat, sending me to Tianmen City.

The Assassination of Liu Zuozhou

Tianjin Correspondence: Liu Zuozhou, the commander of the Third Security Corps of Hebei (formerly known as the First Security Corps of the War Zone), was suddenly attacked at the train station in Fengrun County at 3:50 p.m. on the fourth. He lost too much blood and died that night. His troops are temporarily led by Deputy Commander Li Fengyun, Corps Adjutant Sun Zhenhuan, and Secretary-General Zhang Weixiang. In addition to reporting the details of Liu's assassination to the Pingzheng Review Council, the Military Branch, and the Hebei Provincial Government on the fifth, Li Fengyun and others also publicly recommended Liu's uncle, Liu Lesan (the current commander of the cavalry battalion of Liu's troops), to succeed as the corps commander and requested the province to appoint him. From the evening of the fourth, Fengrun County west to Tangshan and east to Shanhaiguan were placed under special alert. More than eighty Japanese soldiers from Shanhaiguan boarded a special train to Fengrun County at 8:05 p.m. on the fourth to assist in searching for the murderers and were on guard at the station. In Guye, Tangshan, Changli, Fengrun County, and Shanhaiguan, whenever a passenger train arrived at the station, the military boarded the train to search for suspicious persons. Yesterday (the fifth), twenty suspects were arrested in Luan County and detained in the security corps headquarters. The Japanese North China Garrison Army paid extreme attention to this matter. At the same time, Umezu, the commander of the Japanese army who went to Shanhaiguan to inspect the troops, immediately sent Ishii, a senior staff officer of the military headquarters working in Shanhaiguan, to Fengrun County to investigate the truth. Wenjing, the captain of the Tangshan Japanese Garrison, also stayed there to assist in everything. Ikeshima, the captain of the Tianjin Japanese Military Police, rushed to Fengrun County on the morning of the fifth to interrogate the arrested criminals in order to find out the truth of the case. The incident occurred as follows: on the morning of the fourth, Gu Ruzhen took office as the administrative inspector of the Fengshan-Shanhaiguan District in Tangshan. At the same time, Umezu went from Tianjin to Shanhaiguan to inspect the Japanese army. Liu Zuozhou went to Tangshan to participate in Gu's inauguration ceremony and welcome Umezu. At 2:30 p.m., he boarded the train from Tangshan. When Umezu headed east and arrived in Fengrun County, Wenjing, the captain of the Tangshan Japanese Garrison, was in the same car as Liu. After Umezu left with the train, they left the station together. Liu was about to board his own car when suddenly more than ten thugs jumped out of the station and fired and bombarded Liu at the same time, throwing two bombs. Liu was hit by bullets in the chest and waist and fell to the ground. Three of his attendants were also injured. The station security team heard the gunshots and bombings, and the thugs took the opportunity to escape. Stray bullets injured Kitamura, a senior soldier in the Japanese military police auxiliary team who was on duty at the station. For a time, the order at the station was chaotic. Wenjing directed the Japanese military police garrison to assist the security team in arresting the thugs. At that time, three suspicious persons were captured. The injured Liu Zuozhou was carried to the station railway hospital, where he died at 6 p.m. due to excessive blood loss. Fengrun County was placed under curfew that night, the city gates were closed, and telephone lines were temporarily cut off, but the people in the city were still stable. Liu Zuozhou was a native of Gaiping, Liaoning, 33 years old, and a graduate of the tenth class of infantry at the Northeast Jiangwutang. He served as a junior officer in the Northeast Army. During the Rehe Incident, Li Jichun gathered desperadoes and Lao Haozi bandit gangs to disturb eastern Shanhaiguan. After being recruited, Li Jichun was sent away, and Lao Haozi also fled outside the pass. The two units were then reorganized into the First and Second Security Corps of the War Zone. The Second Security Corps was commanded by Zhao Lei, and the Japanese side recommended Liu to serve as the commander of the First Security Corps. Since the new security team of the war zone changed defenses, the Japanese side again requested that Changli and Leting be the defense areas of Liu's troops. Including Fengrun County, the defense area expanded, and the power gradually expanded. The reason for this assassination is unknown, but it is said that Liu Guitang, Qi Wenping, and others gathered bandits outside the Great Wall, wanting to disturb the war zone and demanding that Liu (Zuozhou) cooperate. Liu refused and sent people to incite Liu's troops, but they were captured by Liu. Therefore, they formed a grudge and took action to plot against him, hoping that after Liu's death, the troops would be divided, and then they would take the opportunity to incite them. (6th)

The Yellow Peril is Spreading; The Xiaofu River Breaches Again; Huantai County Suffers Heavy Losses; The Water Level in Shanzhou Rises Suddenly

Jinan Correspondence: The Yellow River in Shandong breached at Dongzhuang in the upper reaches, and the floodwaters spread, affecting more than ten counties in western Shandong, causing a tragic disaster. As the Yellow Peril is spreading, the Xiaofu River in Huantai County, western Shandong, downstream from the Ma Da Lake to the Xiaoqing River, also breached due to excessive rainfall and a sudden rise in accumulated water. Nearby towns and villages were all submerged, and the disaster also affected Changshan County. Wang Yuanyi, the magistrate of Huantai County, has telegraphed the province requesting funds to rescue the disaster victims. Although the water level of the Xiaoqing River in Gaoyuan County has slightly decreased in recent days, it has not yet escaped danger. The special commissioner of the county came to the province to collect sacks, and the Department of Civil Affairs issued them to the commissioner on the third to carry back to the county for emergency repairs.

After the Yellow River in Shanzhou rose sharply on the fourth, it quickly receded. On the fifth, the River Affairs Bureau received a report from the Shanzhou Hydrological Station that at zero hour on the fifth, the water level suddenly rose to 294.14 meters, with a flow rate of 5,850 cubic meters per second, which was very turbulent. The River Affairs Bureau has reported to the provincial government and telegraphed the section chiefs and county magistrates along the river to pay close attention to prevention. On the fifth, the upper and middle reaches of the province also reported rising water levels, while the lower reaches had stable water levels, indicating that the water situation is still serious. (5th)

A Macabre Parricide Case in Songjiang

Zhang Xue, a 64-year-old midwife from the sixth household of the fourteenth jia of the fifth bao in Mojia Lane outside the West Gate of this county, is the wife of the late resident Zhang Zhaosheng. Zhang had opened the Xinghua Village candy store at the entrance of Mojia Lane during his lifetime. Because he had no children, he adopted a son named Shunxi, who is now 22 years old and married to a Wang woman. Unexpectedly, Shunxi became degenerate and showed no ambition. The Zhang couple were deeply disappointed. On the fifth day of the lunar year last year, Zhang, saddened by his son's unworthiness, secretly took an overdose of tranquilizer water and died. Unexpectedly, after Shunxi's father passed away, he became even more reckless, arbitrarily mistreating his wife and elderly mother, and constantly extorting money from his mother. Therefore, the Xinghua Village candy store he opened could not be maintained and was closed. His wife, Wang, also left. Shunxi then associated with loafers and wandered outside. At the end of May this year, Shunxi again extorted money from his mother. When she refused, he severely beat her, causing injuries to her face. She reported it to the Public Security Bureau, which sent him to the County Court for trial on charges of assault and sentenced him to imprisonment for several months, sending him to prison for execution. Until the fifth of this month, Shunxi was released from prison after serving his term. Unexpectedly, at about 12 o'clock that night, two men whom his mother, Xue, did not recognize suddenly came and claimed to invite Xue to deliver a baby. Xue did not think twice and went with them. Before leaving, she entrusted Fang Wenh and Zhang Zhengyou, two people living in the same house, to watch over the door and told them that if the knife was released from prison today and came home to stay, please refuse him. Unexpectedly, less than an hour after Xue left, Shunxi suddenly came with Xue's room key. He immediately opened the lock and searched Xue's room for money and valuables. At that time, the residents asked him where he got the key. According to him, he accidentally met his mother on the road, who gave him the key and told him to go home to sleep. The residents considered that Xue's words before leaving were contradictory and became suspicious. That night, Shunxi stayed in his mother's room. The next day, Xue still did not return home, and Shunxi got up and rummaged through things as usual. The two residents, Fang Wenh and Zhang Zhengyou, became even more suspicious. Therefore, they joined Zhang Yongsheng, the town police officer, to report to the Second Public Security Sub-bureau and requested them to send police to stop him from taking things. The sub-bureau sent police chief Yang Zhiquan. At that time, because his behavior was suspicious, he took Shunxi to the station so that he could be verified after Xue returned home. Unexpectedly, at about 1 p.m. today (the 7th), Zhang Yuanbiao, a direct-action policeman from the station, was passing through a remote place in the second district of Zui Bai Chi South River and suddenly saw several children shouting that a female corpse had been found on the public cemetery. The policeman went to check and indeed saw a female corpse, about 60 years old, with her upper body naked and a cloth belt tied around her throat, lying dead among the trees. It was clear that she had been murdered. The policeman reported it to the Second Sub-bureau. After the corpse was discovered, someone recognized it as Zhang Xue and suspected that her son had murdered her. The sub-bureau telegraphed the Public Security Bureau and the District Attorney's Office to send personnel to examine the corpse. At the same time, Officer Luo ordered Zhang Shunxi to be brought to court for a preliminary interrogation. At first, Shunxi tried to deny that he had murdered his mother, but then he confessed that because he was at odds with his mother and was plotting to get her money, he colluded with two people who were released from prison with him. First, the two men tricked his mother out, and then they strangled her to death with a belt. While speaking, his eyes were fierce, his attitude was arrogant, and he said that there was no need to ask more questions, it was nothing to die. Officer Luo ordered him to be detained. At about 3 p.m., Liu, the prosecutor from the District Attorney's Office, led Wang, the prosecuting clerk, and others to the scene of the corpse in the rain to examine it. After examination, it was determined that the deceased, Zhang Xue, was indeed strangled to death. He filled out the corpse form and instructed Xu Yongqing, the rural policeman of the second district of the river, to guard the corpse so that the family members could come to collect it for burial. The murderer, Zhang Shunxi, was reported by the Second Sub-bureau to the General Bureau for verification.

A Bizarre Death of a Ferry Boat Owner in Wuxi

Fan Aquan, a 34-year-old farmer from Beixingtang in the seventh district, usually operated a ferry boat between Wuxi and Beixingtang and also traded in wheat. Recently, wheat prices fell, resulting in heavy losses. The day before yesterday, at about 10 o'clock at night, Aquan went to Beiyu Lane to collect scattered wheat. He returned to Beixingtang at about 2 o'clock and stayed on the ferry boat. The next morning, at about 7 o'clock, villagers glimpsed Aquan sleeping soundly on the bow of the boat, naked and sunburned without waking up. Everyone thought it was strange. Looking down, they saw Aquan's face was pale, with saliva all over his mouth, and his legs were purple and his flesh was peeling off. Touching him, he was already stiff. There seemed to be rope marks on his neck. Everyone was in an uproar, with various rumors spreading. Some said that Aquan's death was bizarre, perhaps he was assassinated and strangled, and there were knife wounds on his lower body. Fears of a Lack of Autumn Silkworm Eggs in Zhejiang Province

The autumn silkworm season is approaching. This year, Jiangsu Province produced about 800,000 purebred silkworm eggs (1 million rough eggs), while the estimated quantity needed by each county in the province is about 600,000. However, Zhejiang Province needs to purchase about 270,000 from Jiangsu Province. It is estimated that Jiangsu Province will be short of 100,000 eggs. The Jiangsu Provincial Silkworm Industry Improvement Management Committee, to prepare for contingencies, adopted the suggestion of Zhou Yuanxun, deputy director of the Wuxi Model District, and ordered 50,000 autumn silkworm eggs from the association for relief in areas lacking eggs. At the same time, it ordered each district to quickly guide silkworm farmers to order eggs. Each breeding farm was informed that because Jiangsu Province's demand for eggs was pressing, they could only reduce the quantity shipped to Zhejiang by 100,000 eggs, so Jiangsu Province no longer has a shortage of eggs. However, Zhejiang Province estimates that the quantity of autumn silkworm eggs needed is about 500,000 to 600,000, while its output is only about 200,000. The total shortage will reach 200,000 eggs, causing great panic. The Zhejiang Provincial Construction Department is currently discussing remedial measures.

Regulations on Wage for Silk Reeling Workers

The Silk Factory Association of this county held the first second member representative conference yesterday, chaired by Qian Fenghao, to discuss the following matters: the wages of female workers and working hours varied from factory to factory, and a unified method should be specified. It was resolved that from August onwards, the wages for silk reeling should be uniformly set at 4 jiao 2 fen as the standard. Those who do triangular work will change to full work from August 7th. The time is uniformly set at 5:00 a.m. to go to work and 6:30 p.m. to leave work, with a quarter of an hour stop for breakfast and one hour for lunch. The association will notify each factory to follow the instructions immediately. It was also heard that prices in overseas counties and cities have risen. For example, 85-point Ivina silk can be sold for 500 yuan, and 83-point can be sold for 490 yuan. The household silk of 17-point and 75-point can be sold for 440 yuan, an increase of more than 100 yuan compared to the lowest period in the silk market. The current market price of dry hemp is 118 yuan per dan.

All cases of wasteland, extinct households, land without grain, land with too much grain, land with too little grain, and households with grain but no land must apply for registration before October of this year so that they can be corrected, transferred, supplemented with taxes, and exempted from grain at the appropriate time. All fees for supplementing grain, increasing taxes, transfer, general material fees, and official seal fees are waived. The Italian-Abyssinian Peace Hangs by a Thread, London Sources are Pessimistic, the Trilateral Negotiations are Unlikely to Succeed, Economic Sanctions May Be Implemented 65

(London) Generally, people are pessimistic about the situation regarding the Italian-Abyssinian dispute. Italian Prime Minister Mussolini has again ordered the mobilization of two army divisions, indicating his determination to act on his word, regardless of the opposition from the League of Nations. Semi-official sources believe that even if Britain, France, and Italy hold negotiations on the Abyssinian question in Paris, based on the steps agreed upon in Geneva, success is unlikely if Italy is only given economic benefits without compromising Abyssinia's political independence. Conversely, if Italy insists on its current course and wages war against Abyssinia, Britain will be forced to request the League of Nations to impose sanctions on Italy. Well-informed sources believe that only economic sanctions are feasible, such as blockading the Suez Canal. The League of Nations' position on the Italian-Abyssinian issue differs from its position on the Sino-Japanese dispute over Manchuria. Economic sanctions against Italy are still possible today, unlike the inability to effectively reach Japan. Sources in Geneva believe that at that time, all member states of the League of Nations could concentrate their navies to form an international fleet to enhance the effectiveness of the blockade if the League decides to blockade the Suez Canal. (Havas, 6th)

Belgian Senator's Predictions on Future European War, Strongly Advocates Franco-Belgian Military Alliance 67

Brussels According to the Belgian People's Daily, Belgian Senator Toro held a speech at the Senate Foreign Affairs Committee today on the second European War, which mentioned that once war breaks out, Germany will surpass the Franco-Belgian allied forces by 25 to 30 percent in terms of numbers and will far surpass Franco-Belgian forces in terms of military equipment. Finally, Toro advocated strengthening the Franco-Belgian military alliance while actively seeking economic cooperation between the two countries. Belgian Prime Minister Xu Lun neither affirmed nor denied what Toro said, only stating that Franco-Belgian economic negotiations are currently underway. (National News Agency, 7th)

Reactions to French Austerity Measures, Naval Arsenal Workers Strike and Demonstrate, Three Thousand Workers Flock to the County Government, Tearing Down the Tricolor Flag and Replacing It with a Red Flag, Clashing with Military Police and Resulting in Bloodshed 70

Brest, France Since the government promulgated the delegated legal decree on implementing austerity measures on the 17th of last month, civil servants' salaries have been paid at 90% across the board. Upon hearing that this discount method was implemented when paying the first half-month's wages today, arsenal workers suddenly launched a demonstration against the government's measures. Six thousand workers from the factory participated in the demonstration, with three thousand demonstrators, causing disturbances and a serious situation. The demonstrating workers first gathered near the railway, preventing the express train to Paris from departing, ordering the locomotive workers to stop the train, removing the locomotive, and forcing it to return to the factory. They then marched in a group to the county government and gathered in front of it, tearing down the tricolor flag and replacing it with a red flag. County Governor Henry walked alone into the county government courtyard and removed the red flag. The crowd in front of the government shouted loudly and threw bricks at the government's glass windows. At that time, shops in the main streets closed their shop windows one after another. The demonstrating workers then went from the county government to the naval defense bureau, attempting to break in, but were forcibly stopped by the guarding cavalry and regular troops before retreating. A naval military vehicle was burned in the Sadi Carnot Square. The naval headquarters was guarded by gunners and riflemen and was not attacked by the workers. The disturbances did not completely subside until 6:15 pm. After investigation, one worker was seriously injured and died in the hospital. Two patrol team soldiers were seriously injured and several were slightly injured. (Havas, 6th)

Brest, France Workers in the local arsenal, in opposition to the government's delegated legal decree on austerity measures, held a demonstration yesterday when the first half-month's wages were paid in the factory, marching in groups to the county government, the naval defense bureau, and other places, causing disturbances until after 6 pm. It is reported that disturbances broke out again last night. The demonstrating workers set up obstacles near the naval defense bureau but were repelled by the naval gendarmerie. By 11 pm, the local authorities had subdued the workers and restored order to the streets. At that time, a total of twenty people were injured, including thirteen workers, five patrol team soldiers, and two gendarmes, all of whom have been sent to the naval hospital for treatment. Two of the workers died this morning due to their severe injuries. (Havas News Agency, 7th)

Dockworkers Join the Riot

(Paris) Dockworkers in Brest clashed with police last night in a new conflict. Striking workers marched into the city in formation, shouting slogans such as "Down with Laval" and "Long live the Soviets," destroying many windows and burning naval vehicles, and not allowing the rescue team to provide assistance. The center of the chaos was the Siam Road. Demonstrators repeatedly broke through police cordons here, attempting to break into the police station. The gate of the police station has been destroyed by them. When their forces were no match for the police, they set up obstacles but were dispersed by the cavalry. According to a communique issued by the Ministry of the Interior, Brest's security was restored at 8 pm last night. Among the twenty people injured, there were five policemen and two gendarmes. One dockworker who participated in the struggle today has died from his injuries, and the number of minor injuries is more than one hundred. Today, newspapers are full of news of this riot. (National News Agency, 7th)

Brest, France Workers employed by the government's shipbuilding and arsenal have abandoned the construction of the Dunkerque warship today and have rioted, protesting the government's recent austerity plans and wage cuts. At the same time, the arsenal here has also closed its doors, so there are many riots in the streets. Large groups of military police fought fiercely with the workers for an hour before order could be restored to the streets near the arsenal. However, there are still riots on the main road "Siam Road". At least one person has died and many have been injured. The workers want to incite the army and cause a revolution, so the authorities here have declared martial law today. By evening, the battle between the military police and the workers has not subsided. The authorities have arrested a large number of workers. In addition, 1,200 electrical workers and 500 gas workers have also risen up in riot. According to the police station, this disturbance was instigated by the Communist Party. (National News Agency, 6th)

Le Havre, France Machine room staff of the French Atlantic Shipping Company are opposed to a 10% wage cut. Two crew members of France's largest merchant ship, the Normandie, are also among those protesting. (Reuters, 6th)

The Second Step of the French Economic Policy, Lowering the Cost of Living, The Prime Minister Convenes a National Governors' Conference 71

(Paris) French Prime Minister Laval has now convened a conference of governors from ninety states across the country in Paris to demonstrate the methods of implementing the new economic laws and explain the need for these laws. Laval urgently wants the public to understand the advantages of the plan to reduce the cost of living, as wages have already been reduced, the cost of living has to be reduced accordingly. French President Lebrun is currently on vacation but will chair a cabinet meeting on Thursday. The French cabinet will implement a national public works plan to alleviate unemployment and reduce the prices of essential goods. (Reuters, 6th)

Impact on the London Exchange Market

(London) Opposition to France's austerity orders, resulting in riots in Brest, and street fighting in Paris and Toulon, caused the London foreign exchange market, which had just recovered from a recent currency panic, to panic over the franc. The Central Bank's equalization fund had to buy francs in large quantities. Speculators believe that if France has difficulties in cutting salaries, the Netherlands will be even less able to implement salary cuts. Those in the Netherlands who advocate reducing the value of the currency are now rewarded for their efforts, especially in the Rotterdam area. British bankers are not currently worried about the disturbances in France, but they fear that the spread will cause many congressmen to abandon austerity policies. The election period is approaching, so this change is particularly noteworthy. This autumn will be the most difficult period for Prime Minister Laval. According to many people, the fate of the Laval cabinet will depend on Herriot's actions. Herriot is considered by people in Paris to be the protagonist in the French political situation. (Reuters, 7th)

Major Personnel Changes in Japanese Diplomacy, Eliminating the Old and Establishing a New Lineup 72

(Tokyo) Foreign Minister Hirota, who has gained domestic and international trust for his conciliatory diplomacy, believes that if personnel matters within the ministry adopt a well-rounded, warm-hearted approach, the dissatisfaction of the backbone department will be enough to affect morale. Therefore, he has decided to make major adjustments this autumn and has already started preparations. The reason why more than 70 people in the third rank have not yet been promoted is that 30 to 40 diplomats were employed during the good times of Taisho 8 and 9, a number roughly the same as administrative officials. Because of this attitude, there are also old and weak diplomats in the third rank who should be reorganized. On the one hand, there is a fixed number of Chokunin officials, and capable people in the third rank have no way to advance. Therefore, this autumn, Ambassador Takeo Kojiro to Germany, Matsunaga, Aoki, Fujita, Okamoto, Yamazaki, Murakami, Yano, and other ministers, councilors, and consul-level officials, numbering more than a dozen, who have returned home, will be reorganized and replaced by young and energetic people to transform the atmosphere inside and outside the ministry. (Dentsu, 7th)

US-Japan Cartoon Dispute, Instead Draws the Attention of People Across America, US Newspapers Believe Japan's Protest Was Unwise 73

(Washington) After Japanese Ambassador to the United States Saito protested against the cartoon in the fashionable magazine The New Yorker mocking the Japanese Emperor, another unpleasant incident was discovered in the magazine today. In addition to the cartoon, there was another picture titled "Famous Parents," which included famous parents who had children in 1934. The Japanese Embassy believes that although there is nothing wrong with including the Japanese Emperor in this group of ordinary people, it is "too unsightly." At the same time, the Washington Post today drew a humorous cartoon in its satirical column mocking Japan's protest against the aforementioned cartoon. The picture shows Roosevelt pulling a car with the words "Balanced Budget" written on it, and the title is "Another Situation Britain Must Have." Furthermore, Washington newspapers all commented that Japan's protest would do more harm than good to US-Japan relations and was unwise. The Washington Post said that since Japan protested against the cartoon in The New Yorker, newspapers and publications across the United States have reprinted it, drawing the attention of people across the country. If Japan could have tolerated it, not many people would have paid attention to the cartoon. The newspaper said in an editorial that Japanese soldiers believe that protesting will increase the Emperor's divinity and encourage people to sacrifice more for military service, but they do not know that this kind of protest does not have this effect. The Washington Post believes that from the American point of view, this kind of magazine cartoon does not insult Japan or the Japanese Emperor. (National News Agency, 6th)

International Business Telegraph – Special Business Report from Reuters on August 7 –

Gold and Silver The London gold price today was one hundred and forty shillings and five pence, down four and a half pence.

The futures price was also thirty pence one eight seven five, down zero six two five. India and China sold, the United States bought, and the market was stable.

Spot Silver Mount Murray's Silver Futures opened without much change. Because of US purchases in London, the price here was slightly higher.

Exchange Rates US-UK The London foreign exchange market opened stable. The US-UK exchange rate opened at four dollars and ninety-six cents zero six two five, higher than yesterday's US-UK exchange rate closing price by zero six two five. Within the first hour, it rose one two five. At noon, it fell one two five, and it rose again in the afternoon. At 2 pm, the price was four dollars and ninety-six cents three one two five. UK-France France has issued a new economic law, so a riot took place in the Brest area and street fighting occurred in Paris and Toulon. The price of francs was greatly affected. The London authorities used the equalization fund this morning to regulate it. However, the banking sector is still calm. The French exchange rate opened seven points higher and was seventy-four francs ninety-four. There have been no changes since.

Cotton and Wheat US Cotton The New York cotton market, due to the upcoming release of the Department of Agriculture report, is nearing a conclusion. However, the price after opening today is still stable, and the market is quiet. English Cotton The Liverpool cotton market has a stable price today, because the US Department of Agriculture report is about to be released. At one o'clock in the afternoon, the October price was six, one five unchanged.

English Wheat The Liverpool wheat market fell slightly this morning, expressing sympathy for the weakness of the American wheat and grain markets yesterday. At 1 pm, the October price was five shillings and two and a half pence, down seven five.

US Wheat The Chicago wheat market opened lower by half a point this morning due to the decline in Liverpool prices, but soon rebounded to near yesterday's closing price. However, buyers did not take advantage of the rising tide to buy, so the market was stable. Grains had a slight improvement in both near and distant terms after opening this morning.

New York The opening price of New York rubber fell several points due to the low market price in London. British Economic Advisor, Sir Ross, Will Come to China Soon, Scheduled to Depart This Saturday and Arrive in Shanghai in Mid-September, En Route to Japan to Inquire About Attitudes Towards Loans to China 79

(London) Sir Ross, the chief economic advisor to the British government, was recently sent to China to investigate the economic situation. It was learned today that Ross will depart this Saturday, taking the route of Quebec, Canada, to the Far East. He will be accompanied by Mr. Herbert and Mr. Rogers, senior officials from the British Treasury and the National Bank. After passing through Canada, the three will board the Empress of Asia in Vancouver on August 21st and head to Japan to meet with Japanese government officials to discuss the attitude of the Japanese side towards international loans to China. According to the current plan, the three will arrive in Shanghai in mid-September. A member of the investigation team told the Associated Press today that there have been many rumors from the outside in recent weeks, but they will not go to New York or Washington. It is rumored that Ross recently met with the American banking figure Morgan, who is currently here, and they may have discussed Anglo-American cooperation on loans to China. After the team goes to China, Herbert will stay in China as a financial advisor to the British Embassy, while Ross and Rogers will stay in China for about several months. (National News Agency, 6th)

(London) Black, the British aviator who teamed up with Scott to win the British-Australian flying championship, will perform four major flying feats on the 10th of this month, weather permitting: (1) Fly to Cape Town and then fly back to Britain via Cairo. (2) Fly from Britain to Hong Kong and then fly back to Britain. The above flights will be completed within five days. (3) Fly from Britain to Canada and then fly back to Britain to test the possibility of communicating with ships when flying across the Atlantic. (4) The route is currently unknown. The aircraft he will fly will be the same model as the Comet that won the British-Australian flying championship, but with new equipment added. Zhu Hexiang Appointed Minister to Belgium: Zhu Hexiang Departs Yesterday to Assume Post; Pre-departure Remarks Emphasize the Government's Policy of Maintaining Friendly Relations and Striving for Amity between China and Belgium 81

According to the Central News Agency, Mr. Zhu Hexiang, the newly appointed Chinese Minister to Belgium, departed yesterday afternoon aboard the Conte Verde, a vessel of the Italian Mail Steamship Company, to transit through Italy and then proceed to Belgium to take up his new post. Many of Mr. Zhu's relatives and friends went to the dock to see him off. Details are as follows:

Departure Yesterday Afternoon: Minister Zhu boarded the Conte Verde of the Italian Mail Steamship Company at 12:30 PM on the 7th to depart for his new post. Among those who went to the North Bund Wharf to see him off were Zhao Tiezhang, representative of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs' Shanghai Office, Mr. Taillevoix, Counselor of the Belgian Legation, and many of Mr. Zhu's relatives and friends. Besides Mr. Zhou Bofu, the legation secretary who accompanied him, Minister Zhu was also accompanied by his wife, three sons, two daughters, and a servant. Minister Zhu is expected to arrive in Brussels at the beginning of next month to arrange for the early presentation of his credentials.

Statement Released: Minister Zhu stated to reporters from various newspapers before his departure, "I studied in Belgium for seven years and have been back in China for over twenty years. Many of my former classmates in Belgium are now serving in the government. The Prime Minister and Minister of Foreign Affairs, Mr. Meng Qilang, is a graduate of the University of Leuven and was also my classmate. There are also many well-known figures in political, academic, financial, industrial, and commercial circles who are old acquaintances. This time, revisiting that country and meeting old friends will surely be harmonious both personally and for the nation. Moreover, the relationship between China and Belgium has always been strong, and the Chinese in Belgium live and work in peace. Therefore, my visit will be based on the government's main purpose of maintaining friendly relations and striving for amity between China and Belgium. As for the current international situation of our country, many insightful people in the country have expressed their views extensively, so there is no need for me to elaborate. However, I believe that international relations are based on the premise of national interests. We must maintain orderly steps and deal with the situation prudently. If we act impulsively based on temporary emotions, we will surely ruin major events. This is what I deeply hope that my beloved compatriots can deeply research, learn from others' strengths, overcome weaknesses, and strive for self-improvement, which will greatly benefit the future of the country, and our long-cherished aspiration for peace will surely be realized in the future. I will not delay during this trip to Belgium. I will go directly to the port of Venice in Italy to disembark, which will take twenty-three days. I plan to stay there for one or two days and then take a train directly to Brussels, which will take about twenty-four hours. I may take the opportunity to browse the famous attractions along the way. It is expected that the trip will reach Brussels at the beginning of next month. The staff of the embassy will remain the same, so only the First Secretary, Zhou Bofu, will accompany me. In addition, for the convenience of the children's education, the family will also go together."

Minister Zhu and his family photographed before leaving for abroad, by Zhu Shunlin.

Rickshaw Pullers in the French Concession Still on Strike Yesterday: Trade Association Discussed Follow-up Measures Yesterday 86

Rickshaw pullers in the French Concession went on strike the day before yesterday to protest against registration and clashed with Annamese police. Yesterday morning, the strike continued. Rickshaw owners petitioned Du Yuesheng again, and the trade association held a general meeting. The Special District Court interrogated the rickshaw pullers who committed the assault and deflated tires. Details are as follows:

Continued Strike: There are 7,100 rickshaws and 40,000 rickshaw pullers in the French Concession. Since the strike started the day before yesterday, no satisfactory results have been achieved in the negotiations, and a bloody tragedy has occurred. Therefore, the strike continued yesterday morning. Because the rickshaws in the British Concession were deflated, the rickshaw pullers did not dare to go south and only pulled rickshaws in the French Concession. In Hu Nan, except for places accessible by trams and buses, pedestrians had difficulty finding transportation.

French Consul Expresses: Mr. Du Yuesheng believed that the situation of this case was serious and had a great impact on the traffic and security of the Chinese Concession. Therefore, he visited Mr. Badens, the French Consul General, in his personal capacity to discuss appropriate solutions. The French Consul said that the registration of rickshaw pullers did not start with the French Concession. There were precedents in the British Concession. Why did the rickshaw pullers and owners in the British Concession not object, but only opposed the actions of the French Concession? Moreover, the rickshaw pullers committed violence and injured the Annamese police. Therefore, this case is difficult to change. Mr. Du resigned and left.

Du Mediates: At 9:00 PM on the 6th, the Rickshaw Trade Association sent Standing Committee members Gu Songmao, Yu Dajin, Zhang Huaiyang, and Chou Chunshan to Du's residence again to request mediation. Mr. Du said that he had consulted with the French Consul General. The Consul General was very dissatisfied with the rickshaw pullers for beating and injuring the Annamese police. His opinion was that each rickshaw should register one person first, and he would be responsible for resolving everything else to avoid the expansion of the situation and causing social unrest. The rickshaw owners agreed to reply after the meeting.

Injuries: It has been confirmed that the missing rickshaw puller Xue San (i.e., Xue Ruji) was arrested by the police and has been sent to the court. Zhang Jialong and Han Changsheng were seriously injured. As for the three injured Annamese police, (1) No. 233 was injured in the waist, (2) No. 173 was injured in the back. Both of them were seriously injured and unconscious and are currently staying in Guangci Hospital for treatment. (3) No. 480 was slightly injured and was discharged from the hospital after being bandaged.

General Meeting of Rickshaw Owners: The Rickshaw Trade Association held a general meeting of all rickshaw owners at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce at 8:00 AM yesterday to discuss follow-up measures. More than 400 rickshaw owners attended. Rickshaw pullers Xu Hongsheng, Zhou Li, and Wu Yigao attended as observers. Jin Changlin from the Special Zone Office and Li Rujing from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce attended for guidance. Chou Chunshan, Gu Songmao, Zhang Huaiyang, Yu Dajin, Song Yaokun, and other five people served as the presidium. First, Chou Chunshan reported on the negotiations, and then Li Rujing and Gu Songmao delivered speeches.

Court Trial: When the incident occurred the day before yesterday, the French police arrested three rickshaw pullers, Xue Ruji, Li Yuehua, and Xu Xiaosi, and sent them to the Special Second District Court for public prosecution on charges of disturbing order. At 11:00 AM yesterday, Judge Sun Peng, who was authorized, held a trial in the Criminal Eighth Court. After inquiring about their ages and hometowns, he ordered the trial to be postponed to the 14th of this month. At the same time, the police arrested Zhou Guifang, Zhou Peicai, Wang Yongxing, and Zhou Jinhe, who deflated tires, and at 12:10 PM, Judge Sun also tried them in the Eighth Court and ordered the trial to be postponed to 8:00 AM on the 10th of this month.

Authorities Pay Attention: All circles pay attention to this case because it is related to traffic. The Municipal Government, Mayor Wu, believes that this matter is related to security. Therefore, he ordered the Social Bureau to investigate the truth the day before yesterday and ordered the rickshaw pullers to strictly abide by the order and not expand the situation. Yesterday morning, the Social Bureau sent Director Wang Gang and mediator Zhu Guilin to investigate in detail. The bureau will submit the findings to the Municipal Government, and the Municipal Government will formulate solutions based on the bureau's report.

Police Statement: The French police issued a statement yesterday saying that the police can absolutely prove that the Annamese police and reserve police stationed in the Xiejiao area did not open fire on the crowd when the dispute occurred. It is true that the police officers had to fire three shots into the air when the crowd of six or seven hundred people clashed with the Annamese police. (Note: There was no mention in yesterday's newspaper about opening fire on the crowd, so this is a special statement.)

Telephone Bureau Corrects Citizen's Mistake; Fortunately, the Words "Chinese Area" are Not Used 87

In recent years, the Shanghai Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Communications has been refreshing various facilities in its business operations. Recently, when various users printed letterheads and envelopes and included telephone numbers, some added the words "Chinese Area" between the digits. It seems that their intention is to have a relative position with the word "Concession" added to the telephone numbers in the Special Zone. However, I don't know that this kind of measure has a potential impact on international public opinion and public psychology. The bureau realized that this kind of mistake must be corrected as soon as possible, so it specially sent a letter to all users, stating that in the future, when printing letterheads and envelopes and including the telephone number installed by the bureau, the number should be corrected uniformly, and the words "This City" should be added to the number. As for users in the Special Zone, the words "Special Zone" should also be added for identification, etc. It is heard that this letter will be issued to notify all users within the next few days.

Three new bureaus will be established and implemented on September 1. The details are as follows:

Provincial Government Order: Deadline for Abolition

Chen Guofu, Chairman of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, has now received a report from Zhao Dihua, Director of the Finance Department, stating that the original twelve official Shatun property bureaus were established for land reclamation. All expenses are allowed to be withdrawn from 30% of the fair price. It has been two years since the bureaus were established. The income has been decreasing day by day, but the disputes have been increasing day by day. The reason is that each bureau has no fixed expenses. The cunning people arbitrarily commit wrongdoings and repeatedly issue licenses, while the foolish people follow the old rules and procrastinate. Not only is there a way to take advantage of the clearing, but also the more management the more chaotic it becomes. Other factors such as changes in river flow, sand changes, and social and economic decline may also affect income. The director of the Finance Department takes into account the overall situation and originally planned to allocate funds to all bureaus.

Industrial and Commercial Credit Loans: Applicants Should Pay Attention to the Instructions; Applications Will Be Submitted to the Committee for Decision 89

The Industrial and Commercial Loan Review Committee has received about 20 applications since it started processing credit small loans a week ago. It is now conducting investigations and audits and will hold a committee meeting this week to make a decision on lending. However, although the committee entrusted the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to issue instructions with the application forms, most applicants did not pay attention to them, resulting in unclear procedures and frequent errors. Many companies have repeatedly inquired the committee by telephone. Although the committee staff answered them one by one, it is difficult to answer in detail over the phone, and errors are still inevitable. In order for the majority of loan applicants to understand the procedures, the instructions for the loan application are repeated below: Instructions for small credit loans from the Shanghai Industrial and Commercial Loan Review Committee: (1) The total amount is 5 million yuan. (2) Requests for credit loans are limited to factories manufacturing domestic products, stores selling domestic products, and transporters exporting domestic products. (3) In order to enable industrial and commercial enterprises to enjoy benefits equally, the maximum loan amount is limited to 5,000 yuan. (4) The credit loan is (A) for the purpose of maintaining production only and cannot be used to repay old debts, (B) not for speculative business or other improper purposes. Otherwise, once discovered, the committee will report to the government and punish the crime according to the law of embezzlement of public funds, (C) the goods and objects purchased with the loan shall not be mortgaged elsewhere, (D) the borrower shall report the expenses to the committee for reference on a monthly basis. (5) The application form and various forms for the credit loan shall be sent by the committee to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and distributed to the trade associations for the applicants of each industry to fill in and send back to facilitate the process. However, there are too many bureaus, and I am afraid that it will affect the budget. Now, the official properties of each county have been merged into the county. The trend of Shatun is to change the organization. Therefore, it is planned to abolish all the original bureaus and establish three Shatun bureaus to determine the funding and actively clean up. There is no doubt whether it should be liquidated. I will submit a plan, organization charter, and budget and other items, and submit a document for approval. (6) The application form and various forms can be obtained from the committee for investigation and audit on the second floor of the Guohuo Bank on Henan Road and Tianjin Road. Factories and shops that are not members of the trade association can also obtain the above forms from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and send them to the committee for review. (7) If the applicant's own company is already a guarantor of the credit loan, the loan standard amount shall be calculated by combining the amount of the guarantee (for example, if the applicant's qualification can be loaned 10,000 yuan, but there is a guarantee responsibility of 3,000 yuan, then it can only be loaned 7,000 yuan). (8) The committee handles loan investigation matters, and the cost is huge. According to bank regulations, the applicant should be responsible for the investigation fee of 2 yuan to subsidize the cost. The fee will be paid to the committee when the application form is returned, and a receipt will be issued. If the review is unqualified, it will be returned with the receipt. (9) The applicant should pay attention to the various regulations in the loan rules promulgated by the Ministry. (10) The committee may reject any application that does not meet the application procedures and does not comply with the loan regulations. (11) The application form and various forms of the committee are as follows: (1) Application form, (2) Application report, (3) Balance sheet, (4) Profit and loss statement. Regarding the above forms, if the applicant has not filled them out, he can ask those who have experience in new bookkeeping (such as accountants or banking accountants) to fill them out on his behalf.

The case is scheduled to be officially implemented on September 1 of this year. Each bureau should be abolished immediately, and the provincial department should set up a new bureau to handle it in accordance with the newly revised organizational charter. In addition to the detailed abolishment procedures, the Finance Department will issue another order to comply with the order and send it to the outside world. It is also ordered that the director of the bureau comply with the order and quickly sort out and end all documents, drawings, books, registers, etc., prepare a clear list, and prepare to transfer them. The procedures should be completed before August 31. From September 1, the new bureau will start receiving, and no arbitrary delays are allowed. This is very important, remember this order.

Sino-Russian International Relations, Mr. Chen You Talks with Foreign Press Representatives 92

The North China Daily News reports that when the Pacific political turmoil was stirred up by Japan's occupation of Manchuria, Dr. Yan Huiqing, a prominent Chinese diplomat, once said that China had three options: Geneva, Soviet Russia, and Japan. The results of the League of Nations conference greatly disappointed the Chinese people. Later, China and Russia restored diplomatic relations, and Dr. Yan was appointed as the ambassador to Moscow, which has been two years now. On the 6th, Mr. Percy (transliteration), son of Chen Youren, when meeting with representatives of the North China Daily News, talked about the current state of Sino-Russian relations. This is the first exploration of the situation since the two countries resumed diplomatic relations. Mr. Chen believes that this kind of goodwill is still superficial and ordinary. Neither side has obtained special benefits to solidify and sustain it. Take the past fifteen years of Turkish-Russian goodwill as an example. The two countries are connected by a common interest in land, which is the issue of the Dardanelles Strait. Take French-Russian goodwill as an example. Both countries needed to end the European war as soon as possible. It is on this point that they share a common interest. However, there is still no basis for this between China and Russia. In the past eight years, I (Mr. Chen referring to himself) have studied the relationship between China and Russia. What pleases me is that this matter is now in the hands of Mr. Buyanoff (transliteration), the Russian ambassador to China, who can be described with one word: full. The Republic of China's foreign relations, especially with Russia, have experienced extreme harmony (1924-1927) and then armed conflict (1928-1930). The changes have been so drastic due to a lack of mutual understanding. In the past eight years, I have tried my best to bridge the emotions of the intellectual circles of both sides. We can only establish complete goodwill based on the realization of mutual interests. Today, we are still far from this. This interest is certainly ordinary, not special. In international affairs, true goodwill between two countries must be realized only when their special interests have a common point on land in economic interests or political policies. Now, even those who hope that Soviet Russia will cooperate with Japan and other countries on the Pacific Rim are not prepared to point out what special interests these countries have in common. As far as Russia and Japan are concerned, their interests seem to be directly opposed, not to mention common. As for the contact point between Soviet Russia and the United States, it can be summed up with a word from Mr. Bullitt, the American ambassador to Russia, which is "on the Arctic air route that is being crossed." In other words, the interests of the two countries may be the same in the future, but it cannot be said for sure at present. As for the attitude of Soviet Russia towards China, neither the Chinese nor the Russians have shown any inclination towards the contact points that may be sought. I have been observing Soviet Russia and the Russians for more than eight years and know that Soviet Russia is indeed a molecule with potential for seeking peace in the Pacific. The majority of the Russian people are more concerned with building a socialist motherland and raising their own living standards than with carrying out propaganda in other parts of the world. Propaganda, like church missionary work, is a thankless job and certainly has many dangers. According to Mr. Chen, who arrived in Shanghai from Russia three months ago, he has traveled to many cities in North China, as far as Suiyuan. Mr. Chen intends to familiarize himself with other aspects of international relations and China's internal politics and conditions within the next year. For this reason, when he goes to Europe to serve as a special correspondent for the Otsu Mainichi Shimbun, he will first go to Geneva to observe the opening of the League of Nations General Assembly, and then go to major cities to investigate the politics and policies of various countries. Mr. Chen studied in England and also studied at the University of London. He obtained his law degree a week before his adulthood, so he was valued by his teachers and friends. Before returning to China, he worked in the United States and the West Indies. After returning to China, he worked in the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. Later, he was ordered to go to Moscow, which has been eight years now. Mr. Chen is scheduled to take his wife to Europe via Siberia this Saturday, stay for about half a year, and then return to China via the United States.
