May Major Middle Schools and Universities Hold Independent National Goods Exhibitions! 156

— Liu Daozhen

In this year of the "Student National Goods Year" that is raging across the country, the obvious significance of holding exhibitions everywhere is nothing more than the following:

1. To make students realize the importance of promoting national goods: Promoting national goods is, on the one hand, to resist the economic aggression of imperialists and prevent the outflow of rights and interests, and on the other hand, to increase and develop the opportunities for national industries, wash away the shame of material poverty, and create a Chinese machine civilization to realize the thorough success of the Principle of People's Livelihood.

2. To enable students to understand the common sense of national economic geography: The display of concrete national products can give students a little common sense about national economic geography that they cannot get when listening to lectures on foreign economic environment in the classroom. I hope to arouse a curious mind to do a precise research work.

3. To enable students to contact the inner heart of national goods: Those who are usually dressed in foreign clothes, mixed in foreign markets, dyed with foreign ideas, and smoked with foreign air can cool off and wake up your national soul here! You must know that only national goods can show you the spirit of China, and only national products can show you the geographical advantages of China. Improve the shortcomings and develop the strengths. Take this opportunity to work hard to eradicate past mistakes.

However, in the various exhibitions held now, most of them focus on primary schools, browsing around, and do not pay attention to middle schools and universities, which is inevitable. In fact, it is necessary to promote and instill knowledge for primary school students to use national goods, but they are not as deeply intoxicated with Europeanization, fond of modernism, and fond of foreign goods as middle school students and university students!

All middle school students and university students, whether male or female, are mostly in the period of youth and adulthood. They always like to study and adopt imported products for all clothing products. This kind of atmosphere is by no means formed in a single day. Their disease of being intoxicated with Europeanization, despising national products, and not using them can be said to be deeply rooted, which makes people shudder. Therefore, if we do not apply a strong-hearted medicine in this year of "Student National Goods Year" to promote their rapid awakening and recognition of national goods and the use of national goods, there will be no chance to reverse the tide. Therefore, I hope that in the future, the authorities of various middle schools and universities should shoulder heavy responsibilities and devote themselves to preparing an individual national goods exhibition for the school itself, collecting the products of various national goods manufacturers, and often displaying them for browsing. Although there is now a "Student National Goods Year Promotion Federation" holding mobile exhibitions in advance, I am afraid that its whip is too long to reach, and its power is insufficient, making it difficult to achieve universality. If major middle schools and universities can hold their own independent exhibitions, the general students in the school can get the opportunity to know and approach national goods near the water tower, silently move and potentially transform, which is more powerful. As far as I know, a middle school student or a university student who wants to purchase national goods or use national goods often does not know where to buy them to avoid being deceived. They do not recognize the brand names of national goods merchants, nor do they know the trademarks of national products, which leads to a cold heart of trying and hesitates to move forward. The number is not small, which is really regrettable. Therefore, I put forward this question of "May the authorities of major middle schools and universities hold independent national goods exhibitions" for the adoption of the authorities of major middle schools and universities, what do you think?

Opinions on Holding National Exhibition Meetings 157

— Zhang Zhang

Recently, according to newspaper records, national goods exhibitions and national goods sports meetings are being prepared very actively everywhere. It is expected that in the near future, the national goods movement will have a vigorous performance. From the standpoint of the national goods industry, this situation is indeed a phenomenon worthy of rejoicing. However, judging from the situation of national goods exhibitions in various places in the past, I feel that there are several points that should be studied and improved. Now, I will express some opinions of mine for the reference of those who preside over the national goods exhibition:

First, what I want to contribute to the national goods exhibition is the hope that there will be a strict organization and a sound organization. You must know that an unsound organization is the least able to achieve great results. This is the case with anything, and holding a national goods exhibition is naturally no exception. In the past, some national goods exhibitions in various places have been plagued by unsound organizations. For example, it is an undeniable fact that non-national goods were disguised as national goods at a national exhibition in a certain place. Therefore, I very much hope that future national exhibitions must pay close attention to the organizational aspect.

Second, what I want to contribute to the national exhibition is the hope that the selling price of goods in the national exhibition must be equal to the local selling price. Because if it is not like this, it is easy to make the local industrial and commercial circles feel dissatisfied. For example, the opposition of the Zhenjiang business community to the Zhenjiang business operations of the National Goods City Shopping Mall is a very prominent example. Therefore, here, I want to sincerely contribute to the gentlemen who organize the national exhibition, to know that dumping at low prices is the easiest way to cause opposition from local people.

Third, what I want to contribute to the national exhibition is the hope that the rent will be cheap. At present, in general national exhibitions, if manufacturers are willing to participate, the rent for each room must be at least 30 yuan or more. This is certainly not a problem for large-scale national goods factories, but generally small factories do not have the opportunity to participate because of this. In the past, what we saw in the national exhibitions was that the participating national goods manufacturers were all well-known national goods factories, and it was rare for small factories to be able to participate in the question. This situation seems to seek fairness, but the reason why small factories did not participate, in my opinion, is probably because the rent is too high. Therefore, here, I also want to contribute to the gentlemen who preside over the national goods exhibition, and it is also necessary to pay attention to this point. You must know that there are good national goods in small factories, and it is a pity if they do not have the opportunity to participate because the rent is too high.

Fourth, what I want to contribute to the national exhibition is the hope that during the time of holding the national exhibition, more national goods publicity or masquerade speeches will be held to make the general public understand the significance of holding the national exhibition and arouse their interest and determination to purchase national goods.

The above four opinions are what I thought of temporarily. Because the angry wave of holding national exhibitions is rising again recently, I have no regard for the simple publication of Sichuan, and I hope that the wise will not hesitate to teach Zheng, then I am very fortunate.

Organizing "National Goods Purchase Groups" 158

— Lan Shan

"Promoting national goods" is useless if you just talk about it. It is only effective if everyone can speak and act.

Enthusiastic compatriots who support national goods may gather their relatives, friends, or neighbors, as many as they want, and organize a "National Goods Purchase Group." Everyone should encourage each other and strive to not drink non-national beverages, not eat non-national foods, not wear non-national clothing materials, and not use non-national products. The goal is to make all the items seen and touched in the homes of each member of the group purely domestic products. We should treat foreign goods that suck people's blood like mosquitoes and bugs in summer, and use various methods to prevent them from invading and existing in our homes.

When such groups are organized, they can add a lot of fun. Everyone puts the responsibility of supporting national goods on their shoulders, which is a glorious thing! It is also pleasant in one's own heart.

We also hope that in the future, Chinese national goods manufacturers can conduct further research on the manufacture, effectiveness, quality, and price of goods, with the ultimate goal of achieving true "cheap and good quality."

Let's say that consumers and manufacturers should proceed separately and take on their own responsibilities!

County Towns Should Organize National Goods Markets 159

— Yun Sun

Although the capital is the source of the national goods movement, relying on the promotion and advocacy of a few people is biased and insignificant. Metropolitan men and women are excellent members of the national front line, and promoting national goods can achieve twice the result with half the effort. They know how to love the country, they know how to identify domestic products, and each of them has received considerable education and has the ability to read newspapers. People in county towns are relatively backward in everything, their thinking is closed, and their aspirations are often dominated by knowledge. Asking for one or two national product exhibitions is only for half a month. There are not many literate people, and they are unable to identify trademarks. The national goods market is an emerging organization that is unimaginable. In the past two years, only some deformed businesses have been seen in the county town, and some even drive the people to extravagance! A small county town has branches of five or six banks. A person with knowledge, Xi Zhaojia, named it: the world of banks. Following the rise of banks are pawnshops, which cultivate the speculation of the market and the personal theory of getting rich. We should know that enriching the country and enriching the people is the responsibility of the masses. If businessmen are unwilling to work an inch or a foot on the road to enriching the country, and the ignorant people often misunderstand that entertainment can really save the country, they often open several amusement parks in a small city less than three miles away, cultivating the bad customs of the people. In this way, they are invisibly advancing ten feet on the road to national subjugation. I sincerely hope that each county will establish a permanent national goods market, and ask the business leaders and silver money giants of each county to strengthen the strength of the national economy and stand up to establish some reputation in neighboring counties. The party and government authorities should give guidance and supervision. This kind of national goods market should communicate with the national goods organizations in the metropolis. In addition to selling the famous local products of each county, it is necessary to pay attention to household daily necessities and the required cloth for clothes. As for cosmetics and consumables, it is not hoped that they will become the main business in the national goods market in the county. Selling more local products is the fundamental strategy for teaching and helping the inland handicrafts industry. It is much more practical than empty pity for the livelihoods of the unemployed. When the county people have a destination for purchasing domestic products, they do not need other publicity and persuasion. Nantong coarse cloth, Rugao blue cloth, and Shanghai Pudong wool cloth are all examples. I participated in the last meeting of the seventh district of the Shanghai Student National Goods Year Promotion Federation, and there was a proposal that students should be responsible for persuading people to use domestic goods when they return to the inland during the summer vacation. However, many students have the suffering of having no way to persuade people. Who dares to guarantee that the store is purely selling domestic products? This has become a huge problem. I think that preparing for the establishment of a national goods market in the county town is an urgent matter at present. Even rice, wheat, and flour should be sold one by one, because this is a large amount of food, and the flag of non-national goods has long been flying to remote cities. Their footprints are already boundless aggression.

It is really necessary to prepare for the establishment of a national goods shopping mall in the county town. I think that all the temples, civil education centers, or public places in each county are the most suitable places. I hope that enthusiastic people in each county will act quickly. (Editor)

The Credo of National Products Company Employees 161

— Meng Zhao

A country without external enemies will always perish! This sentence means that calamities can revitalize a nation. But look at the pain of China being insulted in recent years? Losing thousands of miles of land, precarious as a pile of eggs! Science is inferior to others, and the nationalistic ideas of our compatriots are inferior to others. The external enemies of our ancient country are enough to cause great pain and suffering! The last effective weapon for revitalizing the country lies in everyone loving and using national products, especially the employees serving in national products companies! They should be like warriors on the battlefield, with only the courage to kill the enemy and defend the country, and absolutely no reason to engage in internal strife! Undermining their own battle lines! Reading about the chaos in a certain national products company in a newspaper, I cannot help but feel worried again. Therefore, I pick up the pen and write "The Credo of National Products Company Employees" below.

(1) Colleagues who have the fate to gather together should be of one heart and mind, unite and cooperate.

(2) Sharing weal and woe, colleagues should eliminate class concepts.

(3) Methods and experience of guiding customers to purchase domestic goods should be discussed together.

(4) Eliminate frivolous behavior between male and female employees, and ban smoking, drinking, prostitution, and gambling.

(5) Employees should jointly adhere to the oath to use national products, setting an example for customers.

(6) Employees should pool their wisdom and offer opinions on selling national products to the manager.

(7) Leaders should eliminate selfishness and be fair and impartial to employees, and should not harbor favoritism or animosity based on hometown or personal relationships.

New News from the National Products Industry in a Week

The Jiangsu Provincial National Products Factories United Association submitted a request to the Ministry of Finance to allocate 20 million yuan to rescue the Jiangsu Province industry, using the factories' income-generating machinery as collateral, and requested a temporary suspension of lawsuits.

The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Construction presided over the convocation of the Provincial Silk, Gauze, Yarn, and Calico Industry Conference, which convened on the first day and resolved many cases.

Shanghai New World National Products World opened on the 5th.

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce's Industry and Commerce Revitalization Committee held its second committee meeting and entertained industry owners.

Minfeng Paper Company adopted the latest foreign methods to imitate cigarette paper, which has been successful. With government approval, it has obtained exclusive manufacturing rights in various provinces and cities.

In recent months, silk and tea exports have been booming, and tung oil exports to the United States have also increased. This is a new phenomenon in the current national products industry.

Education News: The Ministry of Education Approves Provincial Implementation Plans for Compulsory Education: Gansu, Jiangsu, Shandong, Hubei, Zhejiang, Anhui, Henan, and Seven Other Provinces Have Been Approved; Shanghai, Qingdao, and Yunnan Provinces and Cities Are Being Revised 162

(Nanjing Correspondence) Since the Outline of Measures for Implementing Compulsory Education in the 24th Year of the Republic was decided and promulgated by the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Education has actively prepared for the implementation of compulsory education nationwide. First, it formulated the Central Compulsory Education Funding Allocation Measures and announced the allocation of 1.4 million yuan of central compulsory education funding (the 800,000 yuan of Qing Dynasty indemnity subsidy and 500,000 yuan of border education funding have not yet been allocated). In addition, the Implementation Rules for the Measures for Implementing Compulsory Education, the Provisional Regulations for the Annual Short-Term Primary Schools, and the Curriculum Standards for Short-Term Primary Schools have been successively promulgated and ordered to be followed by the Education Bureaus of various provinces and cities. From this, it can be seen that the central government has great determination for compulsory education, which is by no means comparable to the empty talk and perfunctory behavior of the past. The Ministry of Education, for the implementation plans for compulsory education in various provinces and cities in the 24th year of the Republic, in addition to ordering the responsible education administrative personnel of each province and city to go to the Ministry for face-to-face consultation, also ordered each province and city to formulate and submit its implementation plan for compulsory education in the 24th year of the Republic before July 20 for approval by the Ministry and implementation accordingly. As of the time of issuance, the implementation plans for compulsory education that have been approved by the Ministry include Gansu, Jiangsu, Shandong, Hubei, Zhejiang, Anhui, and Henan provinces. The plans of other provinces and cities, such as Shanghai, Qingdao, and Yunnan, have not yet been approved and have been ordered to be revised and resubmitted. In addition, Hebei Province has been delayed due to the relocation of the provincial capital, and the Ministry of Education has approved an extension for submission. By the end of this month, the implementation plans for compulsory education in various provinces and cities across the country should be approved and implemented by the Ministry of Education. The following is a summary of the compulsory education plans of the provinces that have been approved by the Ministry of Education.

Gansu: Class A counties, such as Fugang and eight other counties, will each establish 15 short-term primary schools, totaling 120 schools. Class B counties, such as Wudu and 14 other counties, will each establish 12 schools, totaling 168 schools. Class C counties, such as Wenxian and 45 other counties, will each establish 10 schools, totaling 450 schools. Zhuoni will establish 5 schools. In total, Gansu Province will increase the number of short-term primary schools by 743 in the 24th year of the Republic. The funding and allocation are as follows: the start-up fee is 210 yuan per school, totaling 156,030 yuan; the operating fee is 180 yuan per school, totaling 133,740 yuan. The start-up fee will be raised locally. If the operating fee is insufficient, it will be supplemented by the border education fund and the compulsory education fund allocated from the Boxer Indemnity.

Shandong: In the 24th year of the Republic, 3,270 short-term primary schools will be added, with 6,540 classes, accommodating 261,600 students. The short-term primary schools attached to middle schools and various institutions have a total of 483 classes, accommodating 9,320 students. Private primary schools will be encouraged, with 5 schools in each county, totaling 545 schools, accommodating 21,800 students. By increasing the number of students in existing schools, an additional 319,151 students can be accommodated. The funding will be provided by the central government by appropriating 235,708 yuan from the military advance payments due to the province in the 19th year of the Republic and appropriating 622,207 yuan from the military advance payments repaid by various counties in the 18th year of the Republic to be used as a compulsory education fund.

Hubei: Starting from the 24th year of the Republic, in the first year, the entire province will establish one short-term primary school in each of the 7,502 Lianbao units. In addition, the province will operate 500 schools, totaling 7,002 schools. Wuhan City will add 80 schools. The total number of schools is 7,081, accommodating 708,200 students. In the second year, one more school will be added in each of the densely populated Lianbao units. In the third year, one school will be established in each Lianbao unit. In the fourth year, one ordinary primary school will be added for every 5 to 10 Lianbao units. In the fifth year, one ordinary primary school will be established in each primary school district. The funding in the first phase will be based on a subsidy of 150,000 yuan raised by the province and 100,000 yuan allocated by the central government, totaling 80 schools in Wuhan City and 700 schools in various counties, of which 500 schools will receive 30 yuan per month, and 200 schools will receive a subsidy of 20 yuan per month, with the remaining 10 yuan per month raised locally. The schools established by the Lianbao units in the first year should have 7,000 schools, increasing gradually from the second to the fifth year, so that the compulsory education funding reaches 30% to 40% of the total education funding of the province.

Zhejiang: In the 24th year of the Republic, 1,326 primary schools and 1,242 classes of short-term primary schools should be established, requiring a total of 311,680 yuan. 207,82 yuan will be raised by the central government and the province, and 102,538 yuan will be raised by the counties and cities. The annual expenses of each short-term primary school are 80% for salaries, 10% for supplies, and 8% for office expenses. The average annual expenditure per school is 180 yuan, and the expenditure per class is 80 yuan.

Anhui: There are 2,530,000 school-age children in the province, 310,000 children in school, and 2,220,000 children out of school. 1,200 schools will be established in the first year, 2,400 schools in the second year, 3,800 schools in the third year, 5,400 schools in the fourth year, and 7,200 schools in the fifth year, accommodating a total of 1,600,000 students. In addition, the short-term primary school classes attached to secondary schools can accommodate 200,000 people, and the increased enrollment in various schools is 50,000 people. The conversion of single-grade schools to a two-part system can accommodate 5,000 more people, and the improvement of private schools can accommodate 180,000 more people, totaling 1,480,000 people. The allocation of funds is as follows: In the first year, the central government subsidizes 120,000 yuan, the province raises 170,000 yuan, and the local government raises 150,000 yuan, totaling 440,000 yuan. In the second year, the central government and the province raise 537,000 yuan, and the local government raises 240,000 yuan, totaling 777,000 yuan. In the third year, the central government and the province raise 675,500 yuan, and the local government raises 410,000 yuan, totaling 1,085,500 yuan. In the fourth year, the central government and the province raise 806,500 yuan, and the local government raises 630,000 yuan, totaling 1,436,500 yuan. In the fifth year, the central government and the province raise 905,250 yuan, and the local government raises 905,000 yuan, totaling 1,810,250 yuan. The total is 5,516,9250 yuan.

Henan: There are 3.1 million school-age children in the province, 1.09 million in school, and 1.2 million out of school. About 1 million children should be educated in this period. 190,000 children should be enrolled in the 24th year of the Republic. 1,920 short-term primary schools with 3,840 classes should be established. On average, each county will enroll 1,720 students, and 17 schools with 34 classes will be established. The average compulsory education expenditure for each county is 2,400 yuan. In the 24th year of the Republic, the central government will subsidize 124,400 yuan, the province will raise 134,400 yuan, and the province and counties will raise 177,600 yuan.

Jiangsu: Except for Jiangning Autonomous County, the number of classes to be added in the 24th year of the Republic is 100 classes in the provincial capital's urban area, and 50 classes in each of Lishui, Gaochun, Jiangpu, Luhe, Yangzhou, Yizheng, Jurong, Huaiyin, Yiyun, Donghai and other counties, totaling 500 classes. The remaining 50 counties will each establish 10 to 15 classes, totaling 750 classes. The above will add a total of 1,350 classes. The newly added classes in each county should be at least half of the annual short-term primary schools. The funding for this year will be transferred from the provincial education and youth funding by 100,000 yuan, and 50,000 yuan will be raised from the provincial treasury, together with the central government subsidy of 150,000 yuan, totaling 300,000 yuan. The operating expenses of the newly added classes in each county should be based on the original class expenses of the county. In addition to the provincial subsidy of up to 150 yuan per class, the remaining shortfall will be raised locally. At 150 yuan per class, 50 counties with 750 classes should be 112,500 yuan. The operating expenses for the increased classes in the ten counties of Lishui, etc., will be 300 yuan per class, totaling 150,000 yuan. 100 classes will be established in the provincial capital, at 350 yuan per class, totaling 35,000 yuan. Preparing 1,500 yuan, totaling 300,000 yuan. The start-up costs for the increased classes will be based on the principle of local solicitation or apportionment by the county magistrate, local gentry, and township chiefs. Half of the operating expenses should be used from the county's general reserve fund or education fund. (August 6th)

National Children's Educational Tool and Toy Exhibition to be Held Starting April 4th Next Year 164

The National Children's Year Implementation Committee's general meeting passed the following measures for the National Children's Educational Tool and Toy Exhibition:

1. The purpose of this association: (1) To arouse public attention to educational tools and toys; (2) To encourage the imitation and manufacturing of educational tools and toys; (3) To seek the improvement of educational tools and toys. 2. The exhibits will mainly be domestically produced, and foreign products may also be selected and displayed at the same time for reference. 3. The domestically produced exhibits will be collected by the National Children's Year Implementation Committee from schools, shops, and factories across the country. The reference products will be requested by the association to be sent to the Ministry of Education and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to order overseas embassies and consulates to solicit them from the governments of the United States, Germany, the United Kingdom, France, Russia, Italy, and Japan. 4. The National Children's Year Implementation Committee will hire personnel who have studied elementary school educational tools and children's toys to be judges to evaluate the quality of the products. 5. The standards for evaluating educational tools and toys are as follows: (1) Rich in educational value; (2) Creative in nature; (3) Consistent with science or containing scientific meaning; (4) Sufficient to arouse children's martial spirit (specifically referring to toys); (5) Hygienic; (6) Strong and durable. 6. The National Children's Year Implementation Committee will publish the evaluation results in the newspaper one month after the closing of the exhibition and publish a special edition for reference. 7. The National Children's Year Implementation Committee will request the Ministry of Education and the Ministry of Industry to commend the particularly excellent products. 8. All matters related to the progress of this association shall be handled jointly by the Ministry of Education at the request of the National Children's Year Implementation Committee. 9. The funds for this association will be provided by the National Children's Year Implementation Committee and the Ministry of Education. 10. The exhibition period of this association is ten days, from April 4th to the 14th of the 25th year of the Republic. 11. After the exhibition has been held, the exhibits of this association will be transported to the requesting locations in various provinces and cities for rotational display at the request of each province and city, but all expenses shall be borne by the requester. 12. At the end of the National Children's Year Implementation Committee, the exhibits should be disposed of separately. The products that are requested to be returned in advance will be returned immediately. Those that are not requested to be returned will be established as a permanent museum for preservation. 13. The local Children's Year Implementation Committee may refer to these measures to formulate other measures for holding educational tool and toy exhibitions. The local exhibitions may select one of the two types of educational tools and toys to hold the exhibition. 14. These measures shall be approved and implemented by the Standing Committee of the National Children's Year Implementation Committee.

The Boy Scout Congress That Opened in Switzerland Yesterday Was Attended by 3,500 People 165

—Mr. So-and-so's Speech Scathingly Condemned the Blatant Disregard of International Law by Strong Countries—(Havas Agency, Stockholm, July 7) 3,500 representatives of Boy Scouts from all over the world are now holding a congress here. Today, they gathered at the Olympic Stadium. World Boy Scout Leader Lord Baden-Powell, Swedish King Gustav Adolf, and former Foreign Minister Andet attended and delivered speeches. En's speech stated that the intention of the Boy Scout movement lies in connecting the feelings of various nations and making them friendly to each other, but the current state of international friendship is far from what we hope for. "According to what I have seen, the cruel lessons given to the world by the European War have now been gradually forgotten. The great powers have openly disregarded the principles of international law." This situation is very sad, and so on.

National Boy Scout Disaster Relief Mobilization: The Boy Scout General Association Formulated Four Measures: The Municipal Education Bureau Issued a Circular to All Schools to Comply With 166

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau instructed the public and private primary and secondary school Boy Scout troops in this city, saying: "According to the letter from the China Boy Scout General Association, I hereby inform you that this year's mountain floods and torrents have caused widespread disasters, especially in the Yangtze River and Yellow River basins. Countless compatriots have tragically drowned. Those who were fortunate enough to escape also lost all their property and have no food or shelter. The sorrowful cries of the displaced people can be heard everywhere. Who will come to their aid? The tragic situation is heartbreaking. In view of the Boy Scouts' responsibility to serve and help others, this association has formulated measures for the National Boy Scout Disaster Relief Mobilization and has issued a circular to Boy Scout troops across the country to follow and implement them. In addition to the separate distribution, this letter is hereby sent to you for your information and to instruct the local Boy Scout troops or organizers to comply with them. For the reasons above, a copy of the original measures of the National Boy Scout Disaster Relief Mobilization is attached hereto. All primary and secondary schools and Boy Scout groups are hereby ordered to comply with them." The measures of the National Boy Scout Disaster Relief Mobilization are as follows: A. Work that Boy Scouts should do: (1) Do their best to donate and save pocket money to raise money; (2) Raise cash and solicit donations from relatives, friends, and people in society; (3) Collect supplies. B. Work of the Boy Scout Troop Headquarters: (1) Supervise the Boy Scouts to implement the disaster relief mobilization; (2) Hold entertainment events or sell handicrafts to raise money; (3) Report to the superior authorities and deliver the collected items every week. C. Work of the Boy Scout Leadership Agency: (1) The Provincial and Municipal Councils or the Provincial and Municipal Party Headquarters are responsible for collecting all the donations and items from the troop headquarters and forwarding them to the Boy Scout General Association or sending them directly to the nearest relief association. Then, the handling situation shall be reported to the Boy Scout General Association for record; (2) The Boy Scout General Association is responsible for publicizing this disaster relief mobilization and collecting donations and items to be sent directly to the disaster relief agency. D. Work of the Boy Scouts in the Disaster Area: (1) In addition to self-defense, they should assist the military police and river workers in building dikes and rescuing the endangered; (2) Pay attention to public health, prevent diseases, and take on rescue work; (3) Relieve the refugees, donate clothes, food, and medicine, and try to accommodate them.

Little Men (8) 176

— Originally Written by Ms. Alcott, Translated by Zheng Xiaocang (Zonghai)

"Little darlings, let them have one day in which they can shout, make noise, and laugh to their heart's content. A holiday is not a holiday if it doesn't have a lot of freedom and playfulness. Therefore, they must have one good, unrestrained noise every week," Mrs.裴 often expressed her opinion in this way. People who were generally reserved and strict were surprised to find escalators, pillow fights, and all kinds of unrestrained games in the usually quiet house of Plum Village.

Sometimes, it seemed that the house was in danger of being torn down, but it never happened, because Mr.裴's word could always bring quiet at any time, and the children knew that freedom should not be misused. Therefore, although there were many dangerous predictions, the school flourished on its own, and the students gradually learned etiquette and cultivated their virtues, without anyone knowing how it happened.

Ned felt particularly comfortable at that time. In front of him was a tall porcelain milk jug as a barrier, Pang Tao-mo sat around the corner, and Mrs.裴 was by his side, filling his plate or cup whenever it was empty.

"Who is sitting next to that girl at the other end?" Ned asked his young neighbor lightly during the laughter.

"That is Bai Xiao-qiao. He is Mr.裴's nephew."

"That name is really strange."

"His original name was Qiao-en, but they call him Xiao-qiao because his father is also Qiao-en. But it is written as 'a bridge' Xiao-qiao. It's a joke, don't you think?" Tao-mo said, explaining it patiently. Ned, though not understanding, smiled along and added with particular interest:

"Isn't he a very lovely child?"

"Of course, he is very knowledgeable."

"Who is the fat one next to him?"

"Ah, that is Ke Tai-fei. His name is originally George, but we call him Tai-fei because he eats too much. The little guy next to Uncle Pei is his son, Robert, and that tall freak is his nephew. He also teaches a little, as if taking care of us."

Essays

Snippets 188

— (Voice)

Catching bedbugs must be done in the middle of the night, which shows how prepared people can be. Thus, danger must be drawn when the water and land are level, effort must be made during exams, and practicing skills must be done when suffering losses. Everything can be seen as catching bedbugs at night.

Listening to music is best when it comes from someone else's window in the distance, especially when the singing, whether from a phonograph or radio, suddenly stops and is never heard again, leaving a lingering sound that makes it seem even better.

The worst thing about being human is being at someone else's beck and call: someone sets up a situation and you fall into the trap, being controlled. It is most hateful. To avoid this, you must be like a strategist, carefully considering every move beforehand, or an economist, weighing the importance of every penny. Only then can you cope with life.

Remembering Qiu 189

— Qing Qu

Zheng Qiu was my student thirty years ago, and now I suddenly hear of his death. How can I not be saddened? Recalling the past, we were together morning and night. Sometimes we would talk over a cup of wine, or discuss essays with enthusiasm. It is all like yesterday. When promoting new dramas, we formed the New People's Society. I wrote the explanatory notes for all the plays we produced. Many of them are still in my collection.

At first, the revival of new dramas competed in showing off fashion. There were jokes like Cai Yong wearing a top hat and Tang Yin wearing a braid. Zheng Qiu was not satisfied. He thought it was an insult to celebrities and a reversal of ancient and modern times. How could this be the essence of actors telling stories through their own experiences? So he changed to historical dramas to promote history. The first play was "Wu Song" from Water Margin. At that time, the New People's Society moved to the Tianxian Garden site on Shilu Road. Wang Wuji played Wu Song, Wang Youyou played Ximen Qing, Xu Banmei played Wang Po, Chen Jinghua played Pan Jinlian, Zhang Yeer played Yun Ge, and Zheng Qiu himself played Wu Dalang, whose nickname was Three-Inch Ding Gu Tree Skin. They performed for two nights, labeling the play "Historical Costume Drama" and "Killing the Sister-in-law to Avenge the Brother." Therefore, the box office was very successful for a time.

Later, in the Minming Society, he performed in the play "Hidden Pain." Zheng Qiu played Wang Laoda, adopting a prologue from my "New Shanghai Future Chronicle in Happy World" (Happy World was published in the 30th month of the Republic of China, co-founded by me and Tang Zijisheng, and stopped publishing after the second issue). His sharp words and metaphors for current affairs were so moving that the audience tapped their feet and sighed, penetrating the heart. This can be called a unique path for spoken drama. Although Liu Yizhou and his generation (Liu performed new dramas under the stage name "Wooden Bell") were known for their speeches on stage, compared to Zheng Qiu, they were like the great wizard compared to the lesser one. Later, Zheng Qiu entered the film industry and I parted ways with him. Almost ten years have passed. I was busy with schoolwork and also because of my decline, I practiced quietness and regarded internal reading as my life, and viewed chasing after fame and fortune as a danger. Who knew that our paths would be so different now, and that we would be separated by life and death so suddenly?

Zheng Qiu's life was known to many contemporaries, but from his childhood to his adulthood, I was the most familiar with him. When I have some time, I will write another article to commemorate him, also to write out my heart and to shed old tears. Alas! Zheng Qiu, if you have knowledge, you will surely see it.

The Beef Stall Owner 190

— Chen Liang

When the sun reached the side of the tall chimney of Ewo Factory, the beef stall owner came hurrying over with his heavy load, moaning "Aiyo heng aiyo heng." After all, he was a man in his fifties, and although he was still the same fat man, his energy was limited. Look at his limping steps, it was quite pitiful.

At the mouth of the alley, he put down the load, took off the piece of cloth that had turned gray from white and was stained with oil, revealing chunks of red beef, beef tendon, and beef tripe... He then took out a rectangular wooden board and a gleaming kitchen knife from the wooden bucket behind him. He sat on the wooden bucket and wiped the sweat from his neck, some of which sprinkled on the beef.

An old customer—the drunkard A-he—came running up: "Beef stall owner, cut fifteen copper coins worth of beef, I'll pay thirteen and owe you two." The beef stall owner kept saying, "It's okay, it's okay." He then reached out with his greasy hands to cut the beef, slicing it as thin as mulberry paper. His technique was skilled. He wanted to cut it even thinner, both to satisfy the customer and to avoid losing money himself. He once said to someone, "You can't do business in this market without being a little cunning, or you'll end up losing your wife too."

"Why are your things getting more and more expensive, beef stall owner? You know everything is cheaper now!" The drunkard A-he was dissatisfied. According to his allocation, he wanted to buy four ounces of liquor and take half back to his wife and son for soaking rice. He started eating it, chewing the flavor strand by strand, and then swallowed it.

"Are you still cheating on an old customer? Really, I earn a copper coin to buy medicine. Currently, the foreign exchange rate is over three thousand four hundred, and beef has to be bought with silver dollars. Think about it, doing small business is really not something a human being does." He gritted his teeth. He reached out to wave away the many flies on the beef. One of them followed the drunkard A-he and flew away.

The front of the stall was deserted again. He chatted with the small shoemaker who was packing up his stall, saying that he had a dream yesterday in which he opened a church, but suddenly a fire broke out in the stove... and he woke up in fright. The small shoemaker said to him, "You're going to be a big boss." The beef stall owner smiled bitterly, thinking, "A man who's about to die of old age." He watched the sun go down.

After Reading the Wooden Fish Boat Song 191

— Meng Chuan-an

After reading Mr. Lanshan's Wooden Fish and Dragon Boat Song in this journal, I found that there were some discrepancies between the text and the facts. Based on what I know, I am now making corrections. If you say that I am nitpicking, then that is not my intention.

In the past, those who sang "Wooden Fish Books" mostly beat wooden fish to accompany them. Nowadays, they are replaced with small drums. As the name suggests, the name "Wooden Fish" came from this. The distribution of the story mostly originated from popular folk novels, such as "Regeneration Green" and so on. The plot is nothing more than loyalty, filial piety, chastity, righteousness, joys, and sorrows. Many people in my Guangdong hometown would hold a volume in their hands after tea and wine, singing to their heart's content, as a supreme pastime.

The "Bao Yu Cries at the Coffin" excerpt published yesterday was not a Dragon Boat Song, but a Bangzi slow tempo in Cantonese opera. It was a signature masterpiece of the former young actor Feng Qing-ji. This kind of publication does not belong in the "Dragon Boat" section.

In the past, those who sang "Dragon Boat Songs" were mostly wandering beggars, holding a wooden carved dragon boat in their hands and a small gong drum tied to their chest, singing auspicious dragon boat songs and begging from door to door. Most of them were old women and blind old men, who had no one to rely on. People also pitied them for their old age and were happy to provide for them. Nowadays, new tunes are emerging in the Cantonese opera world. Each new tune incorporates various small tunes, and Dragon Boat song scores are no exception.

"Autumn Regret on the Road" and "Lamenting the Fifth Watch" are famous "Southern Tunes," which were once popular. They are not Dragon Boat Songs. I recall that ten years ago, Mr. Yan Yuechi, the editor of the drama review column of this newspaper, wrote about this. He said that if you don't believe it, listen to Bai Ju-rong sing the Dragon Boat section of "Scolding the Crown Prince" and the "Autumn Regret on the Road" record (produced by Victory Company). The tones are different, and it is easy to distinguish.

There is also a "Cantonese Ballad," which is also one of the folk literatures of Guangdong Province. It was created by Zhao Ziyong's "Night Hanging Autumn Joy," which is sad and charming and was recited for a time. Even today, the Cantonese newspaper industry still has a Cantonese Ballad column to publish such texts to add to the fun.

As for "Saltwater Songs," they mostly involve stories of love between men and women, chasing and answering questions. However, the lyrics are vulgar and not worth taking.

Little Western Paradise 192

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter Seventeen: Do Not Ask About a Daughter’s Body, Hidden Pain Hard to Speak Of, Eagerly Watching the Nobleman’s Face, Together Admiring the Lofty Demeanor

Yueying said, "Master Jia said they are dressed in rags, cannot speak properly, and do not understand etiquette. If they were to run into acquaintances here, it would be very embarrassing, so he doesn't allow them to come." Huanhua stood up and walked to the table, picked up a cup of tea, and slowly drank it, her eyes sizing up Yueying from head to toe. She asked, "Is this the reason you're feeling so down? Is there anything else that's bothering you?" Yueying said, "I've only been with Master Jia for a day; how could I possibly say?" Huanhua smiled, "When a woman is a new bride, her husband always uses sweet words to coax her. Did Master Jia use any sweet words to coax you?" Yueying blushed and smiled slightly. But the smile was very brief, and she immediately stopped and sat with a stern face. Huanhua thought for a moment and smiled, "Do you like Master Jia?" She remained stern. Huanhua said, "Do you hate him?" Yueying said, "Why would I hate him? He didn't seize me; he bought me with money." Huanhua said, "Are you at least a little afraid of him? If you weren't afraid of him, why would you stay inside with the door closed just because he told you to?" Yueying smiled faintly at first, then sighed and said, "I eat their food and wear their clothes; how can I not listen to them?" As she finished speaking, her eyes reddened. Under these circumstances, Huanhua had understood about eighty or ninety percent of the situation. So the two sat facing each other, each silent. For about twenty minutes, neither of them spoke. Then there were footsteps approaching the door, and someone asked, "Huh! Why isn't the door closed?" With this, Jia Duocai came in. (284)

Records of Lingering Fragrance from the Imperial Palace 193

— Originally written by Princess Der Ling of the Qing Dynasty, translated by Qin Shouou

It was roughly like this: For example, if one day she wanted me to do something, even if I felt it was wrong at the time, I still did it according to her wishes because I didn't dare to disobey her orders casually. After it was done, of course, everyone knew it was wrong, but no one dared to criticize it. The Empress Dowager herself would just pretend she hadn't seen it and wouldn't say a word. Then, after four or five days, or six or seven days, when we had completely forgotten about the matter, she would admit it herself.

"That day's matter really was my mistake!" she would always say.

Hearing her say that, I really wished I could say, "That's right, it was your mistake!" But I would never dare to be so presumptuous; I could only think it in my heart.

Now, to speak of the Empress Dowager again, because she didn't want the matter of banishing the Guangdong governor to linger in her mind, causing her to feel unhappy, she was eager to do something more joyful to forget all her troubles. She thought for a long time and finally came up with something.

"These days, the lotus flowers must be blooming profusely; tomorrow morning, there must be hundreds more blooming!" she said to us. "So tomorrow morning, we must all get up especially early and go to Kunming Lake together, take the yacht, and enjoy the scenery to our hearts' content. Everyone remember: we must set off before breakfast!"

Because such an interesting pastime was planned for the next morning, it immediately swept away all the Empress Dowager's worries. Even until she went to bed to rest, she didn't show any signs of irritability or anger. It seemed that even after going to bed, she fell asleep earlier than usual, and she snored frequently, sleeping very sweetly. (384)

Miscellaneous Talk

Random Talk on Goldfish 194

— Wu Jiren

Mr. Chen Youchen, section chief of the Jiangnan Shipbuilding Plant, is very fond of raising goldfish in his spare time. At first, he kept a few tanks to play with in his residence. Later, the fish increased day by day, so last year he gathered three comrades and organized a "Goldfish Paradise Cooperative." On the east side of Dumuqiao Road in western Shanghai, they opened a garden of more than two mu, purchased two hundred sand tanks and twenty cement ponds. The scale is very large, and the collection is especially rich. All kinds of coarse and fine breeds from the north and south are available. Among them, there is a "Five-Colored Dragon-Type Pearl" which can be said to be the champion of all of Shanghai, because this species has never been seen outside. At the moment, the garden opened on the fourth of this month, and Ms. Gu Lanjun, a movie star who also has the beautiful name of "Goldfish Beauty," performed the opening ceremony. Ms. Gu's elegant title was acquired that day at the banquet at Guansheng Farm in Caohejing. On the day of the opening, congratulatory guests and customers were very lively. Mr. Chen plans to set up a retail department after starting business, so the 50,000 to 60,000 small fish harvested this year will surely sell quickly.

Last month, a few fish enthusiasts organized a "Chinese Ornamental Fish Society." Unfortunately, one of the initiators, Mr. Zheng Zhengqiu, fell ill the day after a dinner and passed away in just four or five days. This can be said to be a loss of a leader for our ornamental fish comrades, and it is very regrettable and mournful.

A few days ago, Mr. Xi Guansheng asked me to talk, and he graciously invited me to manage the goldfish at the farm. I said, "Isn't there Mr. Chen Zhongying managing it at the farm?" He said, "He has another job at the factory, and he is also an amateur when it comes to goldfish. He only took care of them before. In the future, we will ask you to handle it, so you can use your expertise." I am very grateful to him, and on the one hand, I can tell my friends that if you have anything to do with goldfish, look for me. I will definitely be at Guansheng Farm every morning.

Recently, I received a letter from Mr. Liang Diancheng of Yangzhou. He told me that he had recently returned from Tianjin and had visited Nankai University in Balitai, Tianjin, to see the goldfish raised in their garden. According to Mr. Liang's letter, "I spent more than eight thousand yuan on raising fish, and I thought I raised them well enough. Who knew that when I saw the fish at Nankai, not a single one of my fish could compare to theirs? Nankai only raises about ten kinds of fish, but they are all exquisite and unparalleled, definitely not comparable to those in the 'Central Park' and 'Western Hills' in Beijing. The bodies of their fish are unusually large, with about three or four hundred that are seventeen or eighteen inches long (equivalent to one foot five inches on a tailor's ruler). The tails are as large as banana leaf fans or large basins, and the bodies are as fat as large rice bowls. The selection of species is even more indescribable. 'Hat-head with everted gills and a ball,' 'Toad-head with everted gills and a ball,' 'Tiger-head with a ball,' 'Telescope-eye dragon with everted gills and a ball,' etc., are not easy to see elsewhere. What is especially mesmerizing is the 'Longevity Star Head with a Mound of Flesh.' The red growth on the top of this fish's head reaches a height of two inches, and unfortunately, there is only one of them. Mr. Liang lingered by the side of the pond, pacing back and forth three or four times, and was reluctant to leave even when it was getting dark. It can be said that he had seen the ultimate." Liang also said that he knew that raising fish was not easy and could not be compared to growing flowers and raising birds, which can be achieved on a small scale. Goldfish are delicate and cannot live mixed in rivers and shores, mingling with the water spirits. Because they have no self-protection ability, Heaven has dressed them in gorgeous brocade scales and transformed them into various beautiful forms to please people. Therefore, fish enthusiasts steal half a day of leisure to admire them. Seeing their swimming joy, their scheming minds gradually disappear, and they forget the hardship of the whole day. And that is how goldfish are able to survive and continue to reproduce. Mr. Liang is truly a connoisseur and can be called the most ardent of fish enthusiasts.

Cotton Yarn: Buying Activity Resumes Due to Rising Standard Price 197

After two days of sharp declines, the yarn market rebounded yesterday. This was due to the standard price breaking through the 900-yuan mark again, which spurred buyers to actively purchase, leading to a gradual increase in market prices. Nevertheless, speculators are collectively buying in, believing that there is a possibility of a rebound since prices have fallen by ten yuan from their peak. Foreign firms, however, are holding steady.

The forward market for standard yarn opened weak, influenced by the previous day's sharp decline. However, prices for distant months were slightly higher. Due to consecutive days of declines, prices had fallen by eight or nine to ten yuan from their peak. Some expected a rebound and a recovery of two to three yuan. The forward market for standard cotton opened weaker, except for the current month. Distant-month new cotton had become significantly weaker after a large sell-off by Daji the previous day. Furthermore, news about US cotton was weak, and prices for each month fell by 0.15 to 0.2 yuan. However, by the third closing, prices rebounded as the gold market recovered, with each month's closing price rising by 0.05 to 0.12 yuan compared to the previous day's closing. In the afternoon session, because the standard price broke through the 900-yuan mark again, sentiment was shaken, and bulls once again added leverage, causing each month to jump up by 0.3 yuan. However, foreign firms remained indifferent, and each month's price rose by 0.15 to 0.24 yuan compared to the morning closing price. Sales figures were: Meiji 1400 dan, Changji 1200 dan, Yuda 2900 zu, Shenchang 2800 dan, Tongxing 2400 dan, Yuan Yi 1800 dan, Changfeng 3700 dan, Yuanxingchang 2800 dan, Hexing 1100 dan, Yichang 1800 dan, Yikang 1000 zu, and Xinheng 1500 dan. Purchases were: Tongfu 2900 dan, Dafeng 2700 dan, Taixing 2200 dan, Xiesheng 1200 dan, Dachang 1900 dan, Shengyuan 3800 dan, Xincheng 1600 dan, Yifeng 1900 dan, and Renfeng 2200 dan. Spot Cotton Consumption is Minimal

Spot cotton consumption is extremely sparse. Factory demand is weak. Incoming sources are estimated to be 1100.

Northern Cotton Crops Affected by Drought

Cotton crops in the provinces of Henan, Shaanxi, and Shanxi were estimated at 1.8 to 2 million dan during the same period last year. This year, current estimates are 1.7 to 2.1 million dan. Due to the severe drought in Shandong and Tianjin, the harvest is estimated to be reduced by half. There is also damage near Jinan. The cotton concentrated near the mouth of the Yellow River, particularly towards Zhangdian, has suffered considerable damage. Recent breaches of the Yellow River near Weishan Lake have only damaged crops like sorghum and soybeans; cotton crops have not suffered any significant losses.

Rumor of Cotton Not Being Shipped to New York Slightly Increases US Cotton Prices

US Cotton Recovers on Short Covering: US cotton opened yesterday with an unstable market and hesitant traders. Prices for each month rose by 4 to 8 points. Positive news from Liverpool and purchases by foreign firms, along with rumors that cotton would not be shipped to New York due to export subsidies, were the main reasons for the slight increase in prices. Subsequently, some retracement occurred, and brokers sold in the afternoon, causing the market to weaken again. The weather remains favorable, but spot demand is sluggish. Textiles have improved. At the close, some short covering occurred, resulting in a stable market. Spot prices rose by 5 points, and futures prices rose by 1 to 6 points. British spot cotton rose by 2 points, while futures prices fluctuated between a decline of 2 points and a rise of 6 points. Indian cotton initially rose due to the strong July White Raw Creek futures, but then fell due to profit-taking by bulls and selling by speculators. Ping Guo Er and Aomura fell by 0.75 rupees. July White Raw Creek rose by 3 rupees, and April-May futures fell by 1 rupee. Original telegram on the left. (6th dispatch)

White Raw Creek Cotton Forecast to Rebound: Another dispatch from Mumbai reports that the opening forecast for April-May White Raw Creek cotton on the 7th is 213 rupees, up by 0.25 rupees from the previous day's close.

US Government Cotton Forecast: New York, 6th: The US cotton's first cotton crop report will be released at noon on the 8th. Based on various private estimates, the forecast production volume is 11,431,000 bales.

Grains: Flour Futures Customers Have Ample Margin for Difficult Times 198

Yesterday, the flour market showed signs of sluggishness. Foreign wheat quotes fell by about 45 jiao in Chicago and rose by 0.1 yuan in Canada. Market sentiment is influenced by the gradual release of current flour stocks by various factories. Although market prices still need to increase by about 0.05 yuan, customers have ample margin, and the standard trend is inevitably being affected. Furthermore, most small investors are being blocked, and factories are slightly hedging, so near and distant months are seeing softer market conditions. However, current wheat market prices are not willing to decline. If foreign wheat orders are unfavorable, there is a possibility of changes. As a result, the current month fell by 0.01 yuan, September fell by 0.025 yuan, October-November fell by 0.075 yuan, December fell by 0.005 yuan, and January fell by 0.075 yuan.

Wheat Market Prices Unlikely to Be Cheap 199

Yesterday, the futures wheat market was generally calm after the morning opening. Chicago foreign wheat was quoted down 45 jiao, and Canada was up 0.1 yuan. However, market sentiment is that the current wheat trend is quite stable. Wheat prices in both local and outside ports show no signs of softening. Therefore, although transactions were not brisk, market sentiment was able to hold steady, mainly because inland wheat merchants are mostly unwilling to take risks by selling futures for distant months. As a result, there were no changes in prices for any month compared to the previous day. The spot wheat market also showed a slight upward trend because local quotes have not changed, and the supply arriving daily is exceptionally weak. Asking prices from various parties are also 0.01 to 0.02 yuan higher.

Oil Market: Wuhan White Tung Oil Continues to Fall - Hongjiang Oil Falls Outside of the Official Market - 202

Wuhan white tung oil prices rose too quickly, and foreign firms were unable to support the market. Last week, prices fell directly from 48.6 yuan per dan to 45.9 yuan. After entering this week, the market remains weak, and prices continue to fall, dropping to 45.2 yuan, then to 45 yuan, and then to 44.9 yuan. It is normal for a sharp rise to be followed by a sharp fall. However, because foreign firms have excessive demand, it is easier to rise sharply than to fall sharply. This current decline is slow and tortuous, because inventories are too thin, and foreign firms are showing signs of trying to buy. Therefore, although prices are falling, the decline is not severe. If foreign firms make more transactions, the price could still jump back to its original level. Therefore, the future market is always easier to rise than to fall. Zhejiang tung oil also follows Wuhan's market, but its fluctuations are not as severe. Last week, Hangzhou traders sold for as high as 39 yuan per stone in Shanghai. Recently, it has also fallen slightly and is now selling for 38 yuan. However, full-weight goods may not be available for less than 43 or 44 yuan.

Hongjiang tung oil should not have fallen in price during the summer sales season due to the reduction in production last year. However, some in the industry are deliberately trying to manipulate the market by selling off at 25.46 yuan per barrel and even as low as 24.8 yuan. However, this is not the official market price and is done for other purposes, intending to attract small profits. However, the market has reached this point, and those unwilling to lose money would rather hold and not sell. It is also heard that those from Hakka do not approve of cheap sales. From this perspective, a turnaround may be easy. July (Commodity Inspection Bureau Report)

Free Talk

An Evaluation of Bazarov 204

— Bai Lai

When we read Arzybashev's Sanin, we always feel that there is a cynical character among the people we encounter over time. When we read Goncharov's Oblomov, we seem to feel that many friends are tainted with that kind of weak-willed and frivolous problem. We can also find Lu Xun's Ah Q from our neighbors, and Cervantes' Don Quixote from travelers from afar. ... The greatest achievement of these many literary archetypes is that they can evoke a sense of intimacy and a vivid sense of reality in readers. At the very least, they always make readers feel that any of the archetypal characters are like friends or enemies they have met before. Based on this significance, let us examine Turgenev's "Fathers and Sons" and Bazarov. Let's see if such a person as Bazarov exists among the masses, and let's try to give him a fair evaluation.

Turgenev's "Fathers and Sons," a history of the conflict between two different generations in Russia in the 1860s, depicts Bazarov, representing the "son" generation, as a nihilist. This can be clearly seen by observing how he argues with Paul, who represents the "father" generation.

"I don't understand you... How can a person not recognize doctrines and rules? What do you base your actions on?" - This is Paul's question.

Bazarov corrected him, "We consider what is useful to be the basis of our actions. At this time, the most useful thing is denial"...

"Deny everything?"

"Deny everything."

"What? Not only poetry, art,... but... it's terrible to say"...

"Everything." Bazarov calmly repeated.

The reason why Russia's great womb was finally able to give birth to a brand new generation should be clearly explained here: It was because Russia had already produced wild characters like Bazarov in the 1860s. Such characters, in any era, are responsible for catalyzing history, and they often inevitably complete a tragic life. Because most people, as Bazarov's opponent Paul said, "They regard all traditions as sacred, they obey elders, they cannot live without faith." However, it is precisely because the lives of these characters are filled with tragedy that they deserve the greatest praise.

Naturally, Bazarov is not entirely without flaws. On the contrary, because he is a vivid character taken from real life, it is obvious that he has flaws. He confessed, "Everything depends on feeling... Take myself as an example. I take a completely negative and denying attitude because my feeling is like this..." This kind of game of idealism also adds to the tragic composition of Bazarov's life.

Therefore, Bazarov is often willful. Although he criticized all the ugliness of reality and slandered all the hypocrisy of society, this tendency should be praised in the sense of accelerating the birth of the old womb. However, he does not demand practice. "I am determined not to do anything," he said. When he answered his opponent, he also made it clear that he just wanted to laugh at everything. From this, we can infer that he is similar to a demagogue in a certain sense, precisely because he does not correctly recognize the reason for his own growth process.

It is because Bazarov has the above-mentioned shortcomings that he is not a person who fell from the sky. Moreover, he is brave, insightful, and he still has the evaluation he deserves. In fact, he is not unaware of his own shortcomings. When his friend Arkady was preparing to get married, Bazarov himself said:

"—At the time of parting, I will say to you again: what you are doing is very clever; because you are not suitable for living our rough, painful, and drifting life. You have no sharpness, no resentment, although you have the courage of youth and the spirit of youth; but it is not enough to do our kind of movement. People of your aristocratic class can at most bear some beautiful patience and express some beautiful indignation, but they can't go beyond this, what is the use! ... But we have to fight. Our dust flies into your eyes, and our sweat splashes all over you,"... This clearly proves that Bazarov has corrected his shortcomings to some extent. Similarly, at the time of his death, he still confessed so modestly.

"...Russia needs me!...No, no, it is obvious that there is no such need. Who is needed? Shoemakers, tailors, butchers"...

However, we should say that we need Bazarov! He lives vividly among the masses, and his shortcomings are even known to us. Because he is not a savior in mythology. His appearance can make us feel his existence clearly. In any case, in this difficult century, it goes without saying that people like Bazarov will still be respected, right?

Knows How to Do Business 205

— Qin Wen

"At the master's house!" This has long become an idiom in my hometown, meaning "you have to make do a little"; because life in your own home is always simpler than in the workplace. When I came back from school, I had to drink river water that always had a muddy taste, and I had to clean the table and mop the floor myself. Even reading a newspaper and sending a letter required me to go out in person. It just so happened that my leather shoe soles had long been worn through and were leaking, so I had to buy another pair of overshoes.

My salary was only enough to cover a little, and I spent a lot on the road, so I planned everything carefully. Before I went out on the street, I asked the people at home what kind of overshoes were good; they all said that it was worth buying the old brand.

When I got to the grocery store, a thin, fair-skinned young man came out to greet me. After he knew what I wanted, he took out a paper box and opened it for me to see.

"I want an old brand," I said, putting the pair of black overshoes back in the box.

"Isn't this an old brand?" the young man said, taking the shoes out again to show me.

"Are there any other old brands?"

"What old brand do you want?"

"Double Coin brand."

"Isn't this it?"

What he was pointing to was the scissors logo; "Double Coin" and "Double Scissors" sounded similar, and the shapes were similar, but they were not the same brand.

"I want Double Coin brand!" I repeated.

"Oh! That's long gone," the young man replied loudly, "There's no Double Coin brand goods anymore!"

"Then what about Da Xi brand or Su Zhu brand!"

"That's even more out of the question; I won't lie to you, sir! This is the best old brand of overshoes now!"

According to my inherent habit, when buying things, I always take the quality into consideration, but I always pay more attention to convenience. As long as it's almost good, I often blur it over. But since I had discussed overshoes with the people at home, I felt embarrassed to be too casual; I thought it might be a good idea to go to another shop to take a look. After expressing that I didn't want the Double Scissors brand, I turned around to leave. The rain was still falling, and the road was very muddy; my toes already felt water seeping in, and it was too difficult to walk on the wet road again. Just as I was hesitating, I suddenly felt a light pat on my shoulder. I turned around to look, and the young man picked up another pair of overshoes and said to me, "This one is the best!"

I took it in my hand and saw that it was the Double Coin brand I wanted.

"How did you just say that this brand doesn't exist now?" I couldn't help but ask him.

"Haha!" he replied triumphantly, "This is really the best old brand! If you want it, I'll sell it to you!"

"Then the Double Scissors brand isn't 'the best?' How did you just say it was the best?"

"Haha! Double Scissors brand is good, Double Coin brand is even better!"

Although he said it very freely, the young man's words were always contradictory; but he also said it in a very serious and energetic way, which made me no longer want to buy from him. The matter was obvious. It was nothing more than because the Double Scissors brand had a higher profit margin, so he wanted to play this trick. Merchants put money first, and lying is not a big deal. It's good to be able to see the wind and steer the boat and adapt to the situation. This young man will always be "successful" in the future; I have no way to name him, so I name him "Knows how to do business."

University Days (4) (0) 206

— By German author Storm, translated by Chen Yin Zhi

She lowered her head, pressing her forehead against the window pane; the white rose was still fragrant on top of her shiny black hair. "He was only a person. In life, he was just a foolish and pitiful man," she said, almost sobbing, "but he was always my father, no one else would love me like he did—if he were alive, he wouldn't reject me now."

After she said this, we were both silent. I unconsciously grabbed her hands, and she let me. Suddenly, I heard from the other side of the room, near the small portico, the 'Count' calling her name.

She trembled all over. "Nali," I said, "Can't you get away from that person?"

She looked at me with wide, melancholic eyes. "I can!" she said softly. I seemed to see a smile appear at the corner of her mouth, but this smile seemed to contain a mysterious element. At this moment, the calling sound rang out again, and it came closer to us.

She quickly wiped away her tears. "Goodbye, Philip, goodbye!" she said in a low voice. I felt her small hands squeeze mine, and then she walked away.

I don't know how long I wandered in the woods. It wasn't until the music in the hall suddenly stopped, allowing me to hear the hooting of an owl in the forest, that I sobered up.

To walk from the stone steps to the path, I still had to pass in front of the house; at that time, I saw Nali once more. She was standing in the corridor, with her arms wrapped around a pillar, looking through the woods towards the sea, where an electric light was dazzlingly reflected on the water.

Seaside

I lay on the mattress, unable to fall asleep for a long time. I was planning how to rely on my mother's help to give Nali a place to live, but the most difficult thing was how to convince Nali to be willing to go there.

I woke up very late the next morning, waking up to see 'Mayor' Fritz—I often called him that when I was young—standing in front of my bed, smiling at me with his honest eyes. Soon we were both sitting on the sofa, and Fritz talked endlessly about our friends in Heidelberg. But I only listened to him with half an ear—the events of last night were still lingering in my mind.

Soon after, at my suggestion, we went out for a walk. We walked side by side along the seaside on the elm tree-lined path, and at this time, I poured out the words that had been accumulating in my chest, telling him what I had heard and seen about Nali. Fritz listened to me in silence, sometimes cursing in a low voice, kicking stones on the road with his feet, or making a stabbing gesture in the air, as if his fist was holding a sword.

This gesture was not without meaning; eight days later, he stood opposite the 'Count' on the dueling field. In the duel, the 'Count' forcefully slashed a sword from left to right, and Fritz was injured in the face; now, when he gets angry, the scar still glows red on his forehead.——

On the Ferry Back Home 207

— Shen Shengshi

With a light heart, I boarded the ferry back to my hometown.

Having been away from my hometown for a long time, now I stepped on the ferry back home again. A kind of indescribable familiar feeling of hometown stroked the heart of a traveler.

On the ferry, I heard the accent of my fellow villagers, which I hadn't heard for a long time.

For half a year, I had been wandering in a small mountain city in northern Anhui for the sake of life, and all I saw was a gray and dilapidated scene. In just this half year, however, I was tired of seeing the sky filled with yellow sand and the dark mountain ridges. In the small mountain city, I was tired of hearing the noisy gongs and drums all day long, the heavy accent; and the life of swallowing sour and spicy dishes with bland steamed buns. From then on, I experienced the bitterness of life.

There were no beautiful mountains and rivers there, and the Huai River rolled with muddy yellow waves; the mountain peaks were bald, and the rugged mountain roads made me tired.

Now stepping on the ferry back home, a stretch of green water, wrinkled with smiling-like soft waves, and the green water spreads out the familiar homesickness. In the distance, the green mountains emerge on the light blue horizon.

Where the smoky trees are broken, there are several farmhouses, and the lush green willows hang upside down on the clear water, and clear cicada sounds float from the willow bushes.

Blocks of fresh green paddy fields floated past before my eyes, and old farmers, with their brown legs bare, were working in the paddy fields.

Along the way, I casually chatted with a former elementary school principal who was on the same boat; he told me that half a month earlier, there had been no rain, and there had been a panic about drought here. Fortunately, it had rained several times in a row, and the fields could be expected to recover!

The ferry sailed along the clear green water, and the lookout tower of my hometown stretched out before my eyes, and I could see it.

There were many female students returning to their hometowns on the same boat, leaning against the window, facing their hometown and singing softly. In a round and soft singing voice, the hometown gradually became visible before my eyes.

The boat reached the pier, and many male and female servants on the shore, with smiling faces, came to welcome the returning masters, young masters, and young ladies!

I thought that in recent years, my family had long since declined with the times, and maids had not been hired for more than two years.

Carrying my suitcase, and with a little sadness, I stepped ashore.

Family 208

— Shengshi

No songs,

No laughter,

The home is like a

broken drum that has long

been silenced,

leaving only a sense of decline.

There used to be days of laughter,

days of easy living.

The home is already in the years of

wind and frost,

declining and dilapidated.

The white chalk walls have long turned dim,

and black bricks are exposed,

like rotten sores on the skin.

The climbing ivy is wildly prosperous,

it strangles the phoenix tree and collapses the wall.

A flower bed of bees has also run away,

like these little creatures,

they have also seen the changes in the family.

Adulthood is accompanied by poverty and worry;

Under the simplest life,

no improper dreams are allowed,

and hope is pitifully thin.

The home is like a broken drum that has long been silenced,

leaving only a lonely melody of loss.

Three Years 209

— Xia Di

Another three years have passed in an instant!

The rapid passage of time really makes people feel a bit flustered, but the original self remains, teaching the wandering heartstrings, playing empty, sad, and famine-stricken melodies. In this vast sea of people, I only encounter nails everywhere, and I have seen enough of many people's cold eyes. Every lively street and quiet alley may have been imprinted with my own footprints, becoming a bubble in the sea of people.

Wandering life has been going on for more than three years, but it has only been three years since I was driven out of the famine in the countryside and became a wanderer in the city. The number of three years accumulated cannot be considered very large, but the wounds are already cutting through this sad heart! A person wanders at the end of the world for a little hope of life, but hope is just like a rope, tightly tightening around your body, saying that you can't move, even if it allows you to move, it's like joking and playing with you. Life is so real.

In these long and short three years, although I have not tasted the bitterness of life universally, people are selfish, who can have a little sympathy for their own kind?

I have heard enough of the roar of the sea breeze, and I am tired of seeing the neon lights of this city, but during the day my wavering heart is like a banner, fluttering and struggling in the flow of illusory dreams. I once used an adventurous eye to inspect the depths of this city, but the deep-hidden, miserable groans require a special perception to listen to those groaning sounds. The misery of life is even worse than the three years I have experienced.

Everywhere is struggling for one's own life, for seeking, but how long is life? The slide of three years is fast. And this invisible time and space is burying its own youth, struggling for three years, it will carry its own desolation to the vast, unknowable future years, stepping into the realm of decay. So, for the past three years of wandering feelings, I recall the taste of olives. However, the dangers of time and the rampant greed disturb people's hearts. When will be the day of sufficiency? I can't help but admire the past three years again!
