Supplement to the Local News Section of Shen Bao

Talking Points

Dispute over the Ban on Coeducation in Ping City 210

— Xing An

The issue of Ping City's ban on coeducation in private middle schools has aroused criticism from all sectors of society, and now the dispute has expanded. On the one hand, the city government insists on not allowing coeducational schools, and has instructed the Social Affairs Bureau to strictly prohibit private middle schools from enrolling female students, and to establish the Second Municipal Girls' Middle School to provide placements for transferred female students. On the other hand, the private middle schools have also submitted a request to the Ministry of Education through the Federation, to stop the Ping City authorities from banning coeducation, and at the same time, they are still enrolling female students. Now the Ministry of Education has sent a telegram to the Ping City authorities with some instructions, but the Social Affairs Bureau has not made the original telegram public due to some reasons. However, it claims that the Ministry of Education, in principle, agrees with the case of single-sex schools. The private middle schools say that the Ministry of Education's reply to the Federation only ordered them to wait for a solution, and did not explicitly say that coeducation is not allowed, and they want to ask the Social Affairs Bureau to read the original telegram. The two sides are currently deadlocked in this dispute.

A country's education system should be unified. Coeducation in middle schools in our country is allowed by the middle school regulations. It has been practiced in various parts of the country for a long time. Unexpectedly, Ping City suddenly took the step of banning coeducation in private middle schools, which is inconsistent with the Ministry of Education's regulations.

Furthermore, if the ban on coeducation in Ping City is implemented, the problem of transferring female students from general private middle schools will inevitably arise in the future. The newly established Second Girls' Middle School enrolls students above the second grade, which is inconsistent with the middle school regulations of the Ministry of Education. Moreover, the original private middle schools in Ping City are divided into commercial and normal departments, while the municipal girls' middle school only has ordinary classes. This will inevitably make it impossible to place female students who transfer. The Ping City authorities should give considerable consideration to this point.

The education sector in our country is really terrible, and in recent years, various meaningless storms have been frequently stirred up. Now the Ping City authorities advocate single-sex middle schools, which is also a superfluous move. According to recent news reports, Guangzhou will also follow suit and implement the ban on coeducation. I don't know if this is because the school spirit in middle schools in Beijing and Guangzhou is particularly bad, so the authorities have to strictly ban it, or is it because the thinking in the north and south is particularly unique compared to other places? However, rectifying the school spirit by separating boys and girls is not a smart way. This can only be regarded as a means of destroying women's education.

Summer Night Grass 211

— Lao Xin

(1) Waves

I once had such an opportunity to relive my dream of a naive wild child in a place where no one paid attention.

It is such a vast desert that you can't see the end of it even if you strain your eyes. This desert is constantly beating, reflecting the faint but shining light that penetrates from the moon, and it is reflected in the roar-like waves. The surroundings are quiet and empty, without any mixed sounds, and the empty echoes dutifully broadcast the waves, chasing the waves, and the magnificent and soft sound of the waves beating against the waves. The desert plays the moving Marseillaise revolutionary song, a tune that yearns for freedom, soaking the entire space. I, an ordinary person, will not be an exception. The unstable floating life of the past year, coupled with the rumors, slanders, and exclusions among friends, has turned me into a silence close to an old man, but at this time, it also becomes active.

So, I straightened my chest that had been wounded by arrows, I spread my pair of powerful arms that I could still be proud of, I faced the waves that were constantly chasing and pointing, I cracked my vocal cords that had been broken by people, and I shouted wildly, like an inhuman wild bull. The magnificent echoes comforted me, and the high tide of the waves encouraged me, making me forget that I was originally hiding in an inconspicuous corner of this man-eating metropolis.

Since I was a child, I have grown up in the arms of the sea. For the sea's majestic appearance, I have worshiped like a religious believer worships his "Lord," and there was a time when I was willing to give everything I had to the sea, let the sea control my future, and turn me into someone like a wave, doing my best responsibility in the whole. The waves seem insignificant; but the waves have done their best for themselves.

——Put your whole body, like a wave, responsibly against the shore! Entrust your whole future to the sea! Turn yourself into the sea, and struggle in the tireless effort to create that magnificent and majestic future!

In this way, I forgot that I was originally a wild child who came out of a high-temperature layer above 100 degrees, and I forgot even more some guys who only seek their own welfare in the "individual" circle and overthrow others, and I forgot even more that this was originally a turbid world, even to the point that I forgot that I was "homeless" on such a night.

Respectable waves, can you think of an ordinary floater's expectations for you?

(2) Shadow

There is no moon tonight, nor are there any stars. The air is as muggy as if it were in a steamer. I can't see any light, and I can't see my shadow.

The one who cares most about me has always been my shadow. No matter what kind of bad environment I am in, or when I am in the poorest time, all my friends leave me, and my shadow still steals a little time to come and visit me, and also brings a ray of light. I think if there is no one in the world who understands me anymore, I will put myself in the realm of silence, let myself be alone, and let the shadow comfort myself.

When I was forced by life to embark on my journey, I also brought a lot of enthusiasm and the heart of a wild child. The road got farther and farther, I saw more liars, and guys who hung sheep's heads and sold dog meat also came to rob me, robbing me of everything I had, and also piercing my heart. In this way, I had to imprison myself in silence again, letting time erode myself. I have not yet embarked on the road contrary to the wishes I had allowed myself at the time, and it is worth thanking the sea and my shadow for constantly stimulating me.

Summer nights are depressing, and everything in the world seems to have become the most cruel thing, and these hypocritical guys only attack some people who have an unfortunate fate and bully them wantonly. In this way, I was injured and hid in an inconspicuous corner, using my own hope to apply to that terrible wound.

——When will I be able to see my shadow?

Interesting; around ten o'clock, the whole village is very quiet. Looking down, only the sun is shining, quietly, without any sound; if there is, it is the crowing of the rooster, which makes it even quieter. The long crowing of the village rooster at noon sounds as if it is lengthening the days. In the loneliness, I sometimes suspect: could it be that the owners are all busy and have left only the rooster to watch the house?

There are only two times when the mountain village is relatively noisy, one is in the afternoon, when the setting sun is about to pass over the mountain, the village women will shout for their children at this time, and smoke will drift out of the roofs. Camels, donkeys, and people are all walking home; naturally, there will be some noise. The other is in the morning. The villagers know that the plan for the day lies in the morning, and they are busy with sound and color, which is also at this time: vegetable sellers go to catch the early market, and young men lead donkeys to the town seven or eight miles away from the mountain to attract tourists: everyone starts with a hope, and being busy in this kind of air is definitely with sound and color.

"Able to Know the Past and Future, Good at Explaining Life and Death, Good Fortune and Bad Luck."—Female Diviner— 212

— Written by Hu Kao

Morning 213

— Lin Xi

——Mountain Residence Miscellany

Although the residence is said to be on the mountain, it is actually not very high; it is not for the sake of escaping the summer heat that I went up the mountain. Not to mention that the houses in high places are expensive, I just feel that there is no need to live so high; cooking for myself, it is inconvenient to go up and down the mountain to buy some scallions and garlic.

Because the residence is not high, the farmhouses in the foothills have become my neighbors. A person who is used to living in the city is living in a foreign village again: the scenery is different from my hometown, and it is very different from the city. For example, in the morning, listening to the donkey's bray, the crows' cawing, and the tinkling of the camel bells going up and down the mountain in the hazy mist, is something I would never dream of in my hometown; in the city, there is still the cawing of crows, but it is difficult to experience the others. In this respect, living on the mountainside is really better than living in a higher place: this is the interest I have only felt after living here for a long time, and I really didn't think of it at first.

There are many mosquitoes in the mountain residence, and many mosquitoes prompt me to go to bed early; going to bed early and getting up early is the only way to live up to the mountain residence. In fact, it is a pity to live on the mountain without experiencing the morning on the mountain. Farmers are mostly busy in the morning, and they are really busy: selling vegetables to attract people to visit the mountains in the town eight miles away: everyone starts with a hope, and being busy in this kind of air is indeed with sound and color.

There is a lot of fog in the mountain mornings, fortunately, it is not very thick, just a layer of gauze, gently covering the houses and trees, and it dissipates when the sun shines on it. Busy people are busy in the fog, showing that what is busy is the sound. The heavy burdens make a creaking sound when pressed on the shoulders, and in the fog, you can only hear the sound and not see the person; when the sound gets louder and farther away, I know that a villager has picked a hope far away. The groaning sound of the donkey driver is with a bit of urging taste, perhaps because the animals are greedy for the wild grass with dew on the roadside. After the urging sound whips away the light fog, the tinkling of the camel bells is much clearer. Let the camel bells drink the song of confidence and move forward step by step, the mountain journey in the morning is not lonely with you on the road; I often say this to the camels in my heart. Really, the camel bells in the morning air will arouse people's confidence and optimism.

Several families in the village know that I and two friends will go to the town to buy vegetables in the morning, and as soon as it is light, they will lead the donkeys to my door. At first, they followed the donkeys, but later, when they got used to it, they simply handed the donkeys over to us.

Page 22

us. When we don't go to town, there will be two or three donkeys tied to the black jujube tree at the door. A friend often says: "Get up, you hear the donkeys kicking the wall again." In fact, it is still very early, and what you see when you push open the window is just fog, it is still early; when the fog is slightly thinner, we ride donkeys around the mountain; it is inconvenient to ride donkeys backwards in the fog, otherwise it might be more interesting. In fact, saying that we ride donkeys around the mountain is more like we are herding donkeys for others: we let the donkeys eat grass and walk; when someone comes to catch up from behind, we pull the reins and let the person in front pass by.

This kind of exercise has made our bodies stronger, and it is still worth living in the mountains; the reason is that we get up early. It is really meaningless to live on the mountain if you get up late; if you don't get up until nine or ten o'clock, will you not be bored to death listening to the lonely long crowing of the village rooster?

Motherhood 214

— Original work by Kato Takeo, translated by Wan Shi

When I was a teacher in an elementary school, one day, in the third-grade classroom, I was lecturing on a lesson in self-cultivation. I forgot what motive I had, but I asked the students: "Everyone! What is in your belly? Do you know?"

When the children were asked, they all raised their hands and answered in unison: "I know! I know!"

One said: "There is rice in the belly." One said: "There is a stomach in the belly." One said: "There are intestines in the belly."

All the children in the classroom gave this kind of answer, and their knowledge was probably limited to this.

So I asked again: "Besides what you have answered, what else is in the belly? Is there anyone who knows?"

None of the children raised their hands to my question. At this moment, in the girls' section, there was a female student named Chuanzi, with a red ribbon tied to her head, and a look of triumph appeared on her face; as if to say that no one could know this question, only she alone could know.

Seeing her expression, I said to her: "Chuanzi, if you know, tell us."

Chuanzi stood up, slightly tilting her head, looking towards me. I saw her cheeks moving slightly, as if she was saying something, but her face was blushing. I didn't hear a word of what she was saying, so I said to her: "I didn't hear you, please say it again!"

Chuanzi's cheeks moved slightly again, and this time, her face was blushing even more; but I still didn't hear her speak, so I said to her again: "Please speak louder."

Chuanzi seemed to have mustered her last bit of courage and said in a murmur: "This... there is a child in the belly!"

When I heard her words, I couldn't help but say: "There is a child in the belly?"

After listening, I smiled slightly. Because of my smile, Chuanzi's face was blushing even more, and even her ears were as red as if they were on fire. She immediately fell into the laughter of the children and became the focus of their eyes. Seeing Chuanzi's expression at this moment, I realized the shyness of a woman, and at the same time, I didn't see her as a girl, but only saw her purity; no! It can be said to be solemn!

Today, on the tram, I accidentally saw a young woman holding a child; because of this young woman, I was reminded of this little story from more than ten years ago. I think Chuanzi must have one or two children now, right? The words she was waiting for back then will now prove their truth in person, right?

Thinking like this, I felt an indescribable joy in my chest.

News 219

The Youth Drama Society attached to the Youth Association was founded by Mr. Tao Dan, Shi Bin, and Shi Chi, three famous figures in Shanghai's Huaguang Foreign Firm, the News and Education circles. The society has been preparing for this for a long time and already has a glorious history and achievements. The internal scale is grand, and high-level male and female members have been selected. It is said that special singing and drama programs will be broadcast on major radio stations in the city soon, and stage performances will be held in major theaters. The society is currently recruiting male and female members for rehearsals of new plays. Anyone who aspires to love music and drama can join the society. A prospectus is available. For mail requests, please attach two cents for postage (blank letters will not be answered). Contact address: Tao Dan, No. 287-291 Guangdong Road, or Shi Chi, No. 41, Lane 685, Gordon Road. In addition, the Beijing-Shanghai Line walking team attached to the society will depart on the 15th of this month and return to Shanghai in early September. It is reported that there are still vacancies. Those who wish to participate should register with Mr. Shi Chi as soon as possible.

Movie News

"Little Angel" Descends to Earth 220

Since Wang Renmei starred in "Song of the Fisherman" at Lianhua Company, there have been no new works released. The people of the country have been eagerly awaiting them, and the descent of "Little Angel" is indeed great news. The original work of "Little Angel" was the first choice for the Jiangsu Provincial Government's education solicitation, written by Jiang Xingde, and written and directed by Wu Yonggang. The plot describes a poor family. The father is on a distant expedition to the country, the grandmother works hard, the mother sews for meager profits, and the daughter cannot attend school due to poverty. The only son is able to study with hard-earned money. However, every member of the family has their own occupation, and family harmony is revealed. Compared to their neighbors who are well-fed and have no fun, the difference is immeasurable. The whole play focuses on the two children, indicating the importance of family education. The richness of emotions can be said to have reached its peak, so the drama's emotional power is extremely great. At the climax of the whole play, the sister saves her brother, sacrificing her own blood. At that time, the air is tense, and the audience is almost breathless and motionless. The emotions are high and unstoppable. The director's skill is amazing. Actors such as Lin Chuchu, Li Junpan, and Tang Tianxiu are all excellent. Hong Weilie's photography and Xu Ke's setting each have their extraordinary achievements. Looking at the whole play, it is impeccable and is indeed an extraordinary work in the Chinese film industry in recent years. The film will be screened in theaters throughout the city recently.

Jincheng Sets Today as Disaster Relief Day 221

All Business Income is Used for Disaster Relief

For the past two months, newspapers have been filled with large-scale news about floods in various places. The extent of the disaster area and the severity of the damage can be said to be unprecedented. The tragic scenes are shocking and unbearable to read. As citizens of China, we should all rise up together and find ways to save the suffering people. For this reason, the Jincheng Grand Theater has set today (Thursday) as Disaster Relief Day. It has specially obtained the consent of Lianhua Film Company and Diantong Company to provide the films "New Woman," "The Highway," and "Peach and Plum Calamity" for free screening in the theater, with one film being shown per showing. All business income for the day, without deducting expenses, will be used for disaster relief. Their enthusiasm for "doing good and giving alms" is worthy of our emulation. I hope all Shanghai movie fans will hurry to participate, because it doesn't cost much (the price remains the same, without increasing). Not only will it benefit the victims, but you can also comfortably watch a two-hour movie in a cool theater. Why not do it? One more thing you should pay attention to is that it's only for today.

Bright Moon Society to Perform "Wild Rose" 222

After performing at the Xinguang Grand Theater last month, the Bright Moon Opera Society is now actively preparing and will stage the large-scale song and dance drama "Wild Rose," which caused a sensation in Shanghai two years ago, at the Central Grand Theater on Six Malu in the city, starting on the 9th of this month. It is reported that the society will be invited to theaters in other cities after this performance. After this performance at the Central Grand Theater, it is feared that they will not be able to meet with the people of Shanghai again in the shortest period of time. Those who love singing and dancing should not miss this opportunity.
